### [1] [Optically Activated Superconductivity in MgB2 via Electroluminescent GaP Inhomogeneous Phase](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20719)
*Yao Qi,Duo Chen,Qingyu Hai,Xiaoyan Li,Xiaopeng Zhao*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 通过在二硼化镁(MgB2)中加入一种能发光的材料(GaP)，并让它在材料内部发光，成功地提升了MgB2的超导转变温度和载流能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探索一种无需改变主要化学成分，即可调控和增强传统声子介导超导体（如MgB2）性能的新方法。

Method: 通过在二硼化镁(MgB2)中引入磷化镓(GaP)电致发光非均相，并在测量时通过偏置电流原位激活其发光，从而研究其对超导性能的影响。

Result: 1. 超导转变温度(Tc)最多提升了约1.4 K。
2. 临界电流密度(Jc)在20K自场下增加了约69%。
3. 不可逆场(Hirr)提升了约31.5%。
这些提升归因于界面光场增强了电子-声子耦合，同时GaP相作为有效的钉扎中心。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种“原位近场增强配对”和“结构钉扎辅助通量优化”协同作用的策略，为构建可由内部光场激活的超导材料系统提供了新的设计思路。

Abstract: Experimental results demonstrate a viable strategy for tuning the superconducting properties of MgB2 through the incorporation of an electroluminescent inhomogeneous phase, revealing an interfacial light-phonon-electron synergistic mechanism that enhances superconductivity in conventional phonon-mediated systems. By introducing GaP electroluminescent inhomogeneous phases into MgB2 and activating their emission in situ through the application of a bias current during measurements, it is experimentally observed that the localized optical field and electromagnetic near field generated at the interface can effectively couple with the E2g phonon mode of the Mg-B layers, thereby significantly enhancing the electron-phonon interaction. As the emission intensity of the inhomogeneous phase increases, the interface light-field-driven mechanism markedly enhances the electron-phonon coupling constant lambda and leads to a gradual increase in the superconducting transition temperature Tc (with a maximum enhancement of approximately 1.4 K), enabling a tunable enhancement of the superconducting pairing channel in MgB2 without altering its primary chemical composition. In addition, the nanoscale dispersed distribution of the GaP inhomogeneous phase is expected to induce fine-scale defects that act as effective pinning centers and promote densification, resulting in an increase of the critical current density by approximately 69% at 20 K in the self-field and an enhancement of Hirr by about 31.5%. These results indicate that the electroluminescent inhomogeneous phase can synergistically enhance the superconducting performance of MgB2 through two mechanisms: "in situ near-field-enhanced pairing" and "structural pinning-assisted flux optimization", thereby providing a new design strategy for constructing superconducting material systems that can be activated by internal optical fields.

</details>


### [2] [Gap Engineered Superconducting Multilayer Nanobridge Josephson Junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20757)
*Giuseppe Colletta,Susan Johny,Hua Feng,Mohammed Alkhalidi,Jonathan A. Collins,Martin Weides*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文实现了一种基于Nb/NbN和Nb/TiN超导叠层的多层三维纳米桥约瑟夫森结，为超导电子学提供了一种可扩展的无氧化物结方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在开发一种可扩展的、无氧化物的约瑟夫森结平台。该平台能够调控超导能隙和邻近效应，同时避免使用聚焦离子束研磨或氧化物隧道势垒等传统工艺。

Method: 使用电子束光刻和氯基干法刻蚀技术，在Nb/NbN和Nb/TiN超导叠层上制造了多层三维纳米桥结构。其中，高电阻率的氮化物层构成了几何弱连接，而顶部的Nb层决定了整体临界温度和薄膜质量。

Result: 成功制造了这些器件，并将其成功集成到直流SQUID（超导量子干涉仪）中，展示了可靠的电路级操作。

Conclusion: 该平台将材料选择性与三维几何结构相结合，为适用于超导电子学的无氧化物约瑟夫森结提供了一条可扩展的路线。

Abstract: We report the realization of multilayer three-dimensional nanobridge Josephson junctions based on Nb/NbN and Nb/TiN superconducting stacks fabricated using electron-beam lithography and chlorine-based dry etching. In this architecture, a high-resistivity nitride layer defines the geometrical weak link, while the top Nb layer sets the overall critical temperature and film quality of the stack. This multilayer design enables engineering of the superconducting gap and proximity effects without relying on focused ion beam milling or oxide tunnel barriers. The devices are successfully integrated into dc SQUIDs, demonstrating reliable circuit-level operation. By combining material selectivity with three-dimensional geometry, this platform provides a scalable route toward oxide-free Josephson junctions suitable for superconducting electronics.

</details>


### [3] [Pressure-Invariant Isotope Effect as Evidence for Electronically Driven Intertwined Order in Pr$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20871)
*Rustem Khasanov,Thomas J. Hicken,Igor Plokhikh,Ekaterina Pomjakushina,Hubertus Luetkens,Zurab Guguchia,Christof W. Schneider,Dariusz J. Gawryluk*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过μ子自旋旋转实验研究了压力对Pr₄Ni₃O₁₀中氧同位素效应的影响，发现SDW转变主要由电子相互作用驱动，而非晶格振动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究的动机是探究三层镍氧化物Pr₄Ni₃O₁₀中自旋密度波（SDW）转变的根本原因，特别是厘清电子-声子耦合在此过程中的作用。

Method: 研究人员使用μ子自旋旋转（μSR）测量技术，对含有两种不同氧同位素（¹⁶O/¹⁸O）的三层Ruddlesden-Popper结构镍氧化物Pr₄Ni₃O₁₀样品施加静水压力，以探究自旋密度波（SDW）转变温度的压力依赖性。

Result: 实验发现在常压下，SDW转变存在微小的同位素位移（¹⁸O样品的转变温度更高）。在静水压力下，两种同位素样品的转变温度均以几乎相同的速率线性下降，导致同位素位移的大小在压力下基本保持不变。

Conclusion: 研究结论指出，由于压力未能增强同位素效应，表明该材料中的自旋密度波转变主要源于电子效应（强自旋相互作用），而非晶格效应。这可能指向一种由强自旋相互作用稳定的、在三层RP镍氧化物中存在的新型交织有序机制。

Abstract: We report muon-spin rotation measurements of the pressure dependence of the oxygen-isotope ($^{16}$O/$^{18}$O) effect on the spin-density wave (SDW) transition in the trilayer Ruddlesden-Popper nickelate Pr$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$. At ambient pressure, the SDW transition shows a finite isotope shift, with $^{16}T_{\rm SDW}=158.04(5)$ K and $^{18}T_{\rm SDW}=159.81(6)$ K. Under hydrostatic pressure, $T_{\rm SDW}$ decreases linearly at nearly identical rates for the two isotope compositions, ${\rm d}\,^{16}T_{\rm SDW}/{\rm d}p=-4.93(5)$ K/GPa and ${\rm d}\,^{18}T_{\rm SDW}/{\rm d}p=-4.90(7)$ K/GPa, such that the isotope shift remains essentially unchanged under compression. The absence of pressure enhancement of the isotope effect points to a predominantly electronic origin of the SDW transition and is consistent with recent inelastic x-ray scattering results, suggesting a new regime of intertwined order in trilayer RP nickelates, which is stabilized by strong spin interactions.

</details>


### [4] [Hopping mechanism for superconductivity revealed by Density Functional Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21417)
*Jose A. Alarco,Ian D. R. Mackinnon*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文分析了MgB2等超导体中的余弦形电子能带，发现其不对称性源于一种跳跃机制，这种不对称性对于理解这些材料的超导性质至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了进一步分析在基于密度泛函理论（DFT）的MgB2电子能带结构中出现的余弦形能带，并探究其与超导机制的关系。

Method: 该研究通过在G-M路径上的特定区间，沿着平行于高对称性G-A方向的倒易方向进行计算。同时，使用包含修正的紧束缚方程，并与无限长原子链的布洛赫轨道 secular 方程进行比较。

Result: 研究发现，费米面附近的能带分裂有利于电子-空穴配对。计算明确显示，一种跳跃机制（hopping mechanism）与余弦形能带的不对称性有关，而这种不对称性与超导能隙和费米面嵌套（Fermi surface nesting）密切相关。

Conclusion: 确定余弦形能带的不对称性，对于解释MgB2、CaC6、LaH10以及许多其他多元素化合物的超导机制具有重要意义。

Abstract: Cosine-shaped bands that occur in DFT-based electronic band structures for MgB2 are further analyzed with calculations along reciprocal directions parallel to the high symmetry G-A direction at regular intervals along G-M. Band degeneracies in close proximity to the Fermi surface (offset from G-A), do not emulate the degenerate bands along G-A. At the Fermi surface, bands split and align favorably for electron-hole pairing with the nodal inflection point located at the Fermi level. Tight-binding equations, including corrections to describe the observed asymmetry of a cosine-shaped band, can be compared to the secular equation obtained for Bloch orbitals of an infinite linear chain of atoms with two s-states. These equations show unequivocally that a hopping mechanism is associated with the cosine-shaped band asymmetry, an asymmetry strongly correlated with the superconducting gap and Fermi surface nesting. Intersections of folded Fermi surfaces and electronic band crossings provide avenues or pathways for electrons from the nested collection to drastically change velocity or momentum, resulting in scattering and disruption of nested, coherent behavior. Determination of cosine band asymmetry, also established for other two element superconductors such as CaC6 and LaH10, is relevant for interpretation of superconductivity mechanisms in many other multi-element compounds.

</details>


### [5] [A possible superconducting gap signature with filling temperature around 40 K in hexagonal iron telluride islands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21959)
*Guanyang He,Yuxuan Lei,Tianheng Wei,Yanzhao Liu,Jian Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 研究人员通过在特定基底上生长 FeTe（碲化铁），在这种通常不被认为有超导性的材料中，发现了接近40K的疑似超导能隙信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 普遍认为 FeTe（碲化铁）不具有超导性，而其近邻 FeSe 则有。本研究旨在探索在特定条件下 FeTe 是否可能表现出超导特性。

Method: 研究团队在 SrTiO3 (001) 基底上生长了具有原子级平坦表面和六方晶格的 FeTe 岛，并使用扫描隧道谱（STS）技术来检测其电子结构。

Result: 研究人员在生长的 FeTe 岛中检测到了一个能隙结构。该能隙的填充温度接近 40 K，其特征类似于超导能隙。

Conclusion: 这项工作表明，通过特定的材料生长方法，有可能在常压下诱导出新的超导体，为探索新型高温超导材料提供了潜在的平台。

Abstract: Superconductivity in the iron-chalcogenide series FeSe-Fe(Te, Se)-FeTe has been restricted to the near neighbor of iron selenide (FeSe), with a general consensus that iron telluride (FeTe) is not superconducting. In this study, we report the method to grow FeTe islands with atomically flat surface and hexagonal lattice on SrTiO3 (001) substrates, in which a gap structure with a gap-filling temperature close to 40 K is detected by scanning tunneling spectroscopy. Such signature is examined under various conditions and reminiscent of a superconducting gap structure. This work might offer a potential platform to explore new superconductors at ambient pressure.

</details>


### [6] [Transparency-controlled multiple charge transfer in superconducting junctions with local shot-noise scanning tunneling spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22145)
*Yudai Sato,Maialen Ortego Larrazabal,Jian-Feng Ge,Ingmar Swart,Doohee Cho,Wolfgang Belzig,Juan Carlos Cuevas,Milan P. Allan,Jiasen Niu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 研究人员开发了一种新的散粒噪声扫描隧道显微镜技术，通过精确控制超导结的透明度，成功观察到电荷输运从单电子隧穿到多电荷转移的演变过程，并验证了相关理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在超导结中，通过散粒噪声测量来量化由安德烈夫反射（Andreev reflections）主导的电荷输运机制，需要对结的透明度进行系统性控制，但这在实验上具有挑战性。

Method: 研究团队开发了一种新型放大器，并将其用于散粒噪声扫描隧道显微镜（noise-STM）。他们利用该设备，在2.2K的温度下对Pb(111)表面进行了测量，并通过调控结的透明度来观察电荷输运的变化。

Result: 实验结果显示，随着结的透明度增加，散粒噪声从单电子隧穿模式演变为多电荷转移（由多重安德烈夫反射引起）模式。这些结果与单通道系统的安德烈夫反射理论模拟在定量上是一致的。

Conclusion: 该研究证实了结的透明度是控制电荷输运演变的关键参数。同时，它也证明了散粒噪声扫描隧道显微镜（noise-STM）是一个强大的平台，能够以原子级的精度和可控的结透明度来研究微观电荷输运机制。

Abstract: Charge transport in superconducting junctions at finite voltages is governed by Andreev reflections, including multiple Andreev reflections, which are processes that enable multiple charge transfer, a hallmark that shot noise can directly quantify. Since the effective charge extracted from shot noise measurements varies with the transparency of the junction, systematic control of transparency is essential but experimentally challenging. Here, we present shot noise scanning tunneling microscopy measurements enabled by a newly developed amplifier, allowing access to different transparency regimes. We perform shot noise measurements on Pb(111) with tunable transparency at 2.2 K and observe that the shot noise evolves from a single electron tunneling regime to multiple charge transfer regime as transparency increases. Our results are quantitatively consistent with theoretical simulations of Andreev reflections and multiple Andreev reflections for a single-channel system. These results establish junction transparency as the key parameter governing the evolution of charge transport and demonstrate that noise-STM is a powerful platform for investigating microscopic charge transport mechanisms with controlled junction transparency at the atomic scale.

</details>


### [7] [Thermodynamic evidence for a pressure-driven crossover from strong- to weak-coupling superconductivity in Pb](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22178)
*Rustem Khasanov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究通过高压实验发现，压力导致元素铅（Pb）的超导性质从强耦合转变为弱耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管热力学临界场 $B_{\rm c}$ 是理解超导凝聚能的关键，但其与压力相关的研究远不如超导转变温度 $T_{\rm c}$ 那样广泛。本研究旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 研究人员使用μSR（μ子自旋旋转/弛豫）技术，在高达约2.3 GPa的静水压力下测量了元素铅（Pb）的热力学临界场 $B_{\rm c}$。通过中间态的磁场分布确定了 $B_{\rm c}(T)$，并从中提取了不同压力下零温时的 $B_{\rm c}(0)$ 值。

Result: 研究发现，$B_{\rm c}(0)$ 的压力依赖性比 $T_{\rm c}$ 更接近超导能隙 $Δ(0)$ 的变化。在较高压力下，$B_{\rm c}(0)$ 和 $T_{\rm c}$ 的对数压力导数趋于一致，表明耦合强度比 $α=Δ(0)/k_{\rm B}T_{\rm c}$ 变得几乎与压力无关。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了热力学证据，证明元素铅（Pb）在压力驱动下经历了从强耦合超导到弱耦合超导的转变。

Abstract: The thermodynamic critical field $B_{\rm c}$ provides direct access to the superconducting condensation energy, yet its pressure dependence has been studied much less extensively than that of the transition temperature. Here, muon-spin-rotation/relaxation measurements of the thermodynamic critical field $B_{\rm c}$ of elemental Pb under hydrostatic pressure up to $\simeq2.3$ GPa are reported. From the magnetic-field distribution in the intermediate state, $B_{\rm c}(T)$ is determined and $B_{\rm c}(0)$ is extracted at different pressures. In combination with previously reported high-pressure data for $B_{\rm c}$ and $T_{\rm c}$, it is shown that the pressure dependence of $B_{\rm c}(0)$ follows that of the superconducting gap $Δ(0)$ more closely than that of the transition temperature $T_{\rm c}$. At higher pressures, the logarithmic pressure derivatives of $B_{\rm c}(0)$ and $T_{\rm c}$ are found to converge, indicating that the coupling strengths ratio $α=Δ(0)/k_{\rm B}T_{\rm c}$ becomes nearly pressure independent. This behavior is interpreted as thermodynamic evidence for a pressure-driven crossover from strong- to weak-coupling superconductivity in Pb.

</details>

### [8] [Competing skin effect and quasiperiodic localization in the non-Hermitian Su-Schrieffer-Heeger chain: Reentrant delocalization, spectral topology destruction, and entanglement suppression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20330)
*Souvik Ghosh*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 这篇论文研究了在一维SSH链中，非厄米趋肤效应与准周期无序之间的相互作用，发现了一个包含五种不同相的复杂相图，其中一个“竞争相”是之前未被报道的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在一维Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) 链中，非厄米趋肤效应（由非互易跳跃引起）与Aubry-André-Harper (AAH) 准周期性无序这两种效应是如何相互作用和影响的。研究者希望理解这两种效应结合时会产生哪些新的物理现象和相变。

Method: 作者使用了多种研究方法来分析该系统。主要包括：精确对角化、传输矩阵分析以及解析相似变换。此外，他们还运用了相位平均诊断、有限尺寸标度分析和数值李雅普诺夫指数计算来验证他们的发现。

Result: 研究绘制了完整的相图，并识别出五个不同的相区，包括一个前所未见的“竞争相区”。在这个竞争相区中，准周期无序会先破坏趋肤效应，然后才使所有态局域化，表现出非单调的逆参与率。研究还推导出了局域化边界的解析表达式，并发现准周期无序会破坏系统的点隙拓扑。此外，结果表明SSH模型的亚晶格结构对于观察到这五种相变至关重要。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了在一个具有亚晶格结构的SSH链中，非厄米趋肤效应与准周期无序之间复杂的相互作用，发现了一个新的“竞争”相，并阐明了其独特的物理特性。研究强调了SSH链的二聚化结构在产生这种丰富相图中的关键作用，为理解非厄米拓扑系统中的无序效应提供了新的见解。

Abstract: We investigate the interplay between the non-Hermitian skin effect and Aubry-André-Harper (AAH) quasiperiodic disorder in a one-dimensional Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) chain with nonreciprocal hopping. By exact diagonalization, transfer-matrix analysis, and an analytical similarity-transformation argument, we map the full ( , $δ$) phase diagram, where A is the AAH modulation strength and the nonreciprocity parameter. We identify five distinct regimes: ( ) topological with extended bulk, (II) AAH-localized, (III) skin-localized, (IV) fully localized, and a previously unreported (V) competition regime exhibiting reentrant partial delocalization, in which intermediate quasiperiodic disorder disrupts the directional skin accumulation before ultimately Anderson-localizing all states. Using phase-averaged diagnostics and finite-size scaling, we confirm that the reentrant regime is robust, characterized by a non-monotonic inverse participation ratio that sharpens with increasing system size. We derive an analytical expression for the modified localization boundary $λ_{c}(δ)=2\sqrt{v_{eff}w}$ with $v_{vff}=\sqrt{v^{2}-δ^{2}}$, which agrees with numerical Lyapunov exponent calculations. We further show that quasiperiodic disorder progressively unwinds the complex spectral loops, destroying the point-gap topology at a critical strength distinct from the band-topological transition ; that the skin effect suppresses entanglement entropy to near-zero values while sufficiently strong AAH disorder partially restores it ; and that the SSH sublattice structure absent in the widely studied non-Hermitian AAH chain is essential for producing the five-phase landscape, as demonstrated by direct comparison with the non-dimerized limit.

</details>


### [9] [Non-Hermitian Disordered Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20393)
*Kohei Kawabata,Shinsei Ryu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 这是一篇关于非厄米无序系统物理学和数学的综述，重点介绍了非厄米随机矩阵理论及其在对称性分类、开放量子系统和临界现象等领域的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米无序系统已成为现代物理学的中心舞台，其影响遍及凝聚态、量子、统计和高能物理等多个领域。此外，这些系统的原理也构成了网络科学、复杂系统和生物物理学等跨学科领域的基础，因为在这些领域中，耗散、非互易性和随机性是普遍存在的。

Method: 本文通过综述的方式，系统性地梳理了非厄米无序系统的理论框架。具体方法包括：1) 介绍其38重对称性分类；2) 引入经典的Ginibre随机矩阵系综并探讨其谱统计；3) 应用该理论分析开放量子系统中的混沌与可积性；4) 研究无序与非厄米性相互作用下的临界现象（如安德森转变）；5) 讨论非线性西格玛模型的有效场论描述。

Result: 这篇综述系统地总结了非厄米无序系统的核心物理和数学框架。主要论点包括：1) 非厄米系统拥有比厄米系统（10重）更丰富的38重对称性分类。2) 非厄米随机矩阵理论是表征这些系统复数谱统计和普适性类的关键工具。3) 该理论在物理学中有重要应用，例如区分开放量子系统中的混沌与可积性。4) 无序与非厄米性的相互作用可导致独特的临界现象，如安德森转变。

Conclusion: 这篇综述全面概述了非厄米无序系统的物理与数学基础，特别是随机矩阵理论的应用。结论是，这个领域是现代物理学的一个核心分支，其原理和工具不仅对理解凝聚态、量子系统等至关重要，也对网络科学、生物物理等跨学科领域具有深远影响。

Abstract: Non-Hermitian disordered systems have emerged as a central arena in modern physics, with ramifications spanning condensed matter, quantum, statistical, and high energy contexts. The same principles also underlie phenomena beyond physics, such as network science, complex systems, and biophysics, where dissipation, nonreciprocity, and stochasticity are ubiquitous. Here, we review the physics and mathematics of non-Hermitian disordered systems, with particular emphasis on non-Hermitian random matrix theory. We begin by presenting the 38-fold symmetry classification of non-Hermitian systems, contrasting it with the 10-fold way for Hermitian systems. After introducing the classic Ginibre ensembles of non-Hermitian random matrices, we survey various diagnostics for complex-spectral statistics and distinct universality classes realized by symmetry. As a key application to physics, we discuss how non-Hermitian random matrix theory characterizes chaos and integrability in open quantum systems. We then turn to the criticality due to the interplay of disorder and non-Hermiticity, including Anderson transitions in the Hatano-Nelson model and its higher-dimensional extensions. We also discuss the effective field theory description of non-Hermitian disordered systems in terms of nonlinear sigma models.

</details>

### [12] [Twist-Induced Quantum Geometry Reconfiguration in Moiré Flat Bands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20849)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在已知的莫尔体系（如扭曲双层石墨烯）中，其量子几何通常继承自单层材料。然而，对于具有复杂能带结构和对称性破缺的系统，这种对应关系是否仍然存在尚不清楚，本研究旨在探讨此问题。

Method: 作者使用紧束缚模型来研究扭曲的双层环流有序戈薇晶格（tb-LCK），并通过调整环流序的相位来观察其量子几何的变化。

Result: 研究发现，扭曲角度可以引发量子几何的重构，并通过能带重构抑制了单层材料的贝里曲率。这种效应源于钒基戈薇材料中固有的强层间杂化，它混合了能量上相距较远的态，从而重塑了量子几何。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在扭曲的双层环流有序戈薇晶格中，其莫尔平带的量子几何不再简单继承自单层材料。这为探索非传统的量子几何提供了新的平台，并指出该系统在钒基戈薇材料中具有实验可行性。

Abstract: The interplay between band topology, Berry curvature, and moiré flat bands lies at the heart of recent advances in quantum materials. In well-studied moiré systems such as twisted bilayer graphene and transition metal dichalcogenides, the quantum geometry of moiré flat bands typically reflects that of the monolayer, with Berry curvature originating from the band edge at the same valley. Whether this correspondence persists in systems with complex monolayer band structures and broken symmetries remains unclear. Here, we study twisted bilayers of loop-current-ordered kagome lattices (tb-LCK), which have been proposed in the context of vanadium-based kagome materials, using tight-binding models, and uncover a twist-induced reconfiguration of quantum geometry. By tuning the phase of the loop-current order, we identify the suppression of monolayer Berry curvature through twist-driven band reconstruction. We attribute these effects to strong interlayer hybridizations, enabled by the unusually large interlayer tunneling inherent to vanadium-based kagome materials, which mix energetically distant states and reshape quantum geometry. These results reveal that twist in tb-LCK suppresses quantum geometric inheritance from the monolayer, and establish loop-current-ordered moiré systems as promising platforms for exploring unconventional quantum geometry in moiré flat bands. We further comment on the experimental feasibility of the proposed system via vanadium-based kagome materials.

Method: 研究人员为扭曲的二分晶格异质双层结构（特别是骰子晶格和石墨烯）开发并分析了紧束缚模型，重点研究了子晶格选择性的层间隧穿（层间杂化）如何产生平带的量子几何。

Result: 研究证明，层间杂化可以在零能量处产生孤立的平带，其数量可通过扭转角度调节。最重要的是，这些平带展现出由层间杂化直接产生的显著贝里曲率和量子度规，达到了陈绝缘体级别。

Abstract: Flat bands in moiré superlattices provide a fertile ground for correlated and topological phases, governed by their quantum geometric properties. While the valley-based paradigm captures key features in select materials, it breaks down in a growing class of systems lacking valley structure, where exotic phenomena such as twist-angle-tunable numbers of flat bands emerge. In this work, we develop and analyze tight-binding models for twisted heterobilayers of bipartite lattices, with a focus on the role of interlayer hybridization in generating flat-band quantum geometry. We demonstrate that sublattice-selective interlayer tunnelings in twisted dice lattice and graphene heterobilayers induce isolated flat bands at zero energy, whose number is tunable by the twist angle. Most importantly, these flat bands exhibit finite Berry curvature and a quantum metric of the Chern-insulator scale, generated through interlayer hybridization. This establishes a mechanism to induce quantum geometry in moiré flat bands beyond the valley paradigm. Our results chart a route to flat-band quantum geometry engineering in twisted bilayer bipartite lattices, with potential material realizations in oxide heterostructures, molecular lattices, and synthetic quantum matter.

No superconducting transition was observed down to the base temperature of approximately 10 mK. This suggests suppression of superconductivity in high mobility quasi-two-dimensional SrTiO$_3$ electron gas, likely linked to vertical confinement and electronic orbital rearrangement. Abstract: We investigate the equilibrium magnetization in ferromagnetic nanoscrews (NSw) using micromagnetic simulations. These systems consist of elongated three-dimensional magnetic membranes with helicoidal geometry, combining curvature, torsion ($\mathrm{w}$), and eccentricity ($ε$) along their length. We focus on the influence of these geometric parameters, together with membrane thickness and inner diameter, on remanent states and coercive fields. Our results, obtained over a broad range of eccentricities and torsions, reveal bistable magnetic behavior, with vortex-domain-wall propagation during magnetization reversal. We identify four degenerate configurations of a remarkably stable mixed remanent state. The coercive field is found to increase with eccentricity for structures with a major axis (larger inner diameter) approximately 30\% larger than the minor axis (smaller inner diameter), while remaining largely insensitive to variations in torsion. These findings are interpreted in terms of geometry-induced modifications of surface magnetostatic charges on the membrane mantle. Overall, our results demonstrate that nanoscrews exhibit robust bistability under systematic geometric deformation, together with enhanced coercivity, highlighting their potential for applications in three-dimensional nanomagnetism.

### [18] [Semiclassical Wave-Packet Dynamics in Phase-Space Geometry: Quantum Metric Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21262)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子几何在凝聚态物理中至关重要，但现有理论缺乏一个能同等处理实空间和动量空间几何的统一框架。本文旨在填补这一空白，发展一个更全面的理论来描述量子几何效应。

Method: 作者基于普朗克常数ħ（等效于空间导数）的展开，建立了一个统一处理实空间和动量空间几何的通用形式主义。利用此框架，他们推导出了波包能量、贝里联络和相空间态密度的量子度规修正，并进一步构建了一个动力学方程。

Result: 研究成功推导出了由量子度规引起的对波包能量、贝里联络和相空间态密度的修正。此外，还发现了一个由度规梯度诱导的极化现象，以及一个源于度规混合分量的线性霍尔响应。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的框架为探索同时存在实空间和动量空间量子几何的系统中的热力学和输运性质提供了坚实的基础。

Abstract: Quantum geometry governs a wide range of transport and optical phenomena in quantum materials. Recent works have explored analogue electromagnetism and gravity in terms of the quantum geometric tensor, whose real and imaginary parts correspond to the quantum metric and the Berry curvature. By treating real- and momentum-space geometries on an equal footing, we develop a comprehensive and general formalism based on an expansion in $\hbar$, equivalent to an expansion in spatial derivatives. We derive the quantum-metric corrections to the wave-packet energy, the Berry connection, and the phase-space density of states, similar to the field-induced corrections in nonlinear response. A kinetic equation that captures quantum-metric effects across the full phase space then follows naturally. We further identify a polarization induced by gradients of the metric and a linear Hall response originating from its mixed components. Our framework provides a foundation for investigating thermodynamic and transport properties in systems where real- and momentum-space quantum geometries coexist.

Abstract: We perform a differential resistance study in the hydrodynamic regime of electron liquid in GaAs/AlGaAs quantum wells. Result: 实验发现，跨平面热导率和载流子双极扩散率在金属-绝缘体相变时均发生剧烈变化。虽然面内（in-plane）电阻显示出大的磁滞现象，但跨平面的热和电荷传输却几乎没有磁滞。这种差异被归因于相变过程中纳米级畴渗透的各向异性。

Here, frequency-domain thermoreflectance (FDTR) of an epitaxial NdNiO$_3$ thin film reveals a sharp change in out-of-plane thermal conductivity across the metal-insulator transition. Complementary frequency-domain photoreflectance (FDPR) reveals a large change in ambipolar diffusivity of photoexcited carriers. While the in-plane electrical resistance shows large hysteresis, out-of-plane thermal and charge transport shows negligible hysteresis. We attribute this discrepancy to anisotropy in the percolation of nanoscale domains across the transition as the film thickness approaches the domain length scale. ### [25] [Floquet generation of hybrid-order topology and $\mathbb{Z}_2$-like bipolar localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21954)
*Koustav Roy,Latu Kalita,B. Tanatar,Saurabh Basu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过对一个二维高阶拓扑模型进行周期性驱动和引入非互易耦合，成功地诱导出了边界态与角态共存的混合阶拓扑相，并实现了一种可控的非厄米趋肤效应。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 1. 周期性驱动能激活一阶拓扑，使系统进入一个同时存在一阶导电边界态和高阶角态的“混合阶拓扑相”。

Abstract: Higher order topology, in the form of the emergence of corner modes, is observed in two dimensions when crystalline symmetries are superposed on the Altland-Zirnbauer classification of topological insulators. It occurs in Benalcazar-Bernevig-Hughes (BBH) model on a 2D square lattice, which owing to an embedded $\mathbb{Z}_2$ gauge field, features a bulk quadrupole moment with localized zero-energy corner states. Further, as a dividend, the BBH model transmutes the general notion of the space-time inversion ($\mathcal{PT}$) symmetry and behaves as a spinful system, without having to invoke `real' spin degrees of freedom. A two-fold engineering of the model, namely a periodic drive, followed by a non-reciprocal hopping render intriguing consequences. As a first, the drive activates first-order topology, and the resulting Floquet phase hosts a coexistence of first-order conducting edges at both zero and $π$ quasienergies along with higher order corner states, which qualifies the coexisting state to be denoted as a hybrid-order topological phase. Further, inclusion of non-reciprocal couplings features a $\mathbb{Z}_2$-like skin effect which demonstrates a drive-induced transition from a unipolar to a bipolar localized phase, and is evidenced via the generalized Brillouin zone (GBZ) theory. While depiction of a GBZ in 2D is challenging, a corresponding 1D map is still possible and can be implemented by exploiting the mirror symmetry. We further uncover conditions under which the skin effect is completely suppressed in our system. Putting together, our results manifest an efficient technique to dynamically engender and control Hermitian and non-Hermitian topological features, that remain otherwise masked in a static scenario.

Inspired by this, we demonstrate a solid-state realization of CISS in an engineered InAs/GaSb quantum well where geometric chirality and dephasing can be introduced controllably. *Matan Bocarsly,Indranil Roy,Weifeng Zhi,Li-Qiao Xia,Aviram Uri,Yves H. Kwan,Aaron Sharpe,Matan Uzan,Yuri Myasoedov,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Trithep Devakul,Pablo Jarillo-Herrero,Eli Zeldov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究在螺旋三层石墨烯（HTG）中发现了一种由电子相互作用驱动的新型“跷跷板”式相变，该相变允许通过掺杂来控制电子的自旋、谷和子晶格这三个内部自由度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在魔角石墨烯体系中，电子相互作用会打破自旋和谷简并性，从而产生对称性破缺的基态。本文旨在探索螺旋三层石墨烯（HTG）中由相互作用驱动的独特性质。

Method: 实验上，研究人员使用了扫描纳米SQUID磁力测量技术来探测磁信号，并辅以输运测量。理论上，他们进行了自洽的哈特里-福克计算来揭示电子能带的重组机制。

Result: 研究人员探测到了一系列尖锐的磁性信号，这与“跷跷板”式的相变一致，即占据和未占据的价带与导带随着掺杂反复交换。这些相变发生在金属性区域，伴随着一种新颖的磁滞现象，但在输运测量中信号微弱。计算表明，电子相互作用重组了所有八个低能平带，导致轨道磁化强度的突变。

Conclusion: 这项研究确立了螺旋三层石墨烯（HTG）是首个可以通过电子相互作用和掺杂来控制全部三种内部自由度（自旋、谷和子晶格）的体系，并引入了一类新的关联相变。

Abstract: In moiré graphene systems, electronic interactions lift spin and valley degeneracies, leading to symmetry-broken ground states. In helical trilayer graphene (HTG), we uncover a distinct interaction-driven mechanism in which the roles of sublattice-polarized valence and conduction bands are cyclically reversed. Using scanning nano-SQUID magnetometry, we detect a series of sharp magnetic signatures consistent with seesaw-like transitions, where occupied and unoccupied valence and conduction bands interchange repeatedly with doping, accompanied by a novel form of magnetic hysteresis. These transitions occur entirely within metallic regimes and leave only weak fingerprints in transport measurements. Self-consistent Hartree-Fock calculations reveal that interactions reorganize all eight low-energy flat bands, driving abrupt changes in orbital magnetization. Our results establish HTG as the first system where electronic interactions provide doping-controlled access to all three internal degrees of freedom - spin, valley, and sublattice - introducing a new class of correlated phase transitions.

</details>


### [28] [Spin Elasticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21981)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的物理学观念认为弹性是材料介质所独有的属性。该研究旨在挑战这一局限，探索弹性是否也存在于自旋这一基本自由度中。

Method: 论文通过理论构建，引入了“自旋弹性”（spin elasticity）这一全新概念，用以描述自旋形态（spin morphology）发生的可恢复形变。

Result: 研究结果揭示了自旋空间中确实存在弹性。这种“自旋弹性”是一种内在机制，主导了自旋结构的形变与恢复。

Conclusion: 该研究得出结论，弹性并非物质世界的专利，而是一种贯穿物质与自旋领域的普适原理。这一发现补全了经典弹性理论的版图，并预示着弹性研究将进入一个超越传统界限的新范式。

Abstract: Elasticity has long been regarded as a property exclusive to material media. Here we uncover its hidden existence in the spin degree of freedom. We introduce spin elasticity-an intrinsic mechanism that governs recoverable deformation of spin morphology. This discovery reveals a previously unrecognized universality: elasticity operates in both matter and spin spaces, underpinning structural integrity across physical realms. By establishing the missing spin counterpart, this work completes the elastic picture and points toward a broader paradigm where elasticity transcends its conventional boundaries.

</details>


### [29] [Nonlinear suppression of dispersion broadening of ultrashort spin-wave pulses in thin YIG films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22051)
*K. O. Nikolaev,D. Raskhodchikov,J. Bensmann,I. V. Borisenko,E. Lomonte,L. Jin,R. Schmidt,J. Kern,S. Michaelis de Vasconcellos,R. Bratschitsch,S. O. Demokritov,W. H. P. Pernice,V. E. Demidov*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究人员在纳米厚度的钇铁石榴石（YIG）薄膜中，通过实验研究了前向体自旋波短脉冲的非线性传播特性。

Result: 实验证明，自旋系统的非线性可以有效抵消色散展宽，形成包络孤子。在微米级的YIG系统中，仅需毫瓦级别的微波功率即可实现孤子。研究人员成功将3纳秒的自旋波脉冲无失真地传输了50微米。

Conclusion: 该研究结果为在微型自旋波电路中实现不受色散效应影响的高速信息传输提供了一种有前景的方法。

Abstract: We study experimentally the nonlinear propagation of short pulses of forward volume spin waves in nanometer-thick YIG films. We show that nonlinearity of the spin system can efficiently counteract dispersion broadening of the pulses, leading to the formation of envelope solitons. We demonstrate that in microscopic YIG systems, microwave powers of the order of one milliwatt are sufficient to reach the soliton formation threshold. At powers slightly above this threshold, we achieve transmission of 3-ns spin-wave pulses over distances of up to 50 micrometers without increase in their temporal width. Our results demonstrate a promising way towards high-rate transmission of information in microscopic spin-wave circuits unaffected by detrimental dispersion effects.

### [30] [Landau-Level-Resolved Mode Mixing and Shot Noise in Gate-Defined Graphene Quantum Point Contacts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22111)
*Shakthidhar Vilvanathan,Jerin Saji,Kristiana Frei,Jakub Tworzydlo,Manohar Kumar*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 这篇论文通过模拟和测量散粒噪声，发现在石墨烯量子点接触中，零朗道能级表现出独特的法诺因子 F=1/3，这与高能级的 F=1/4 混沌极限有明显区别，为区分不同传输机制提供了新方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子霍尔效应下，仅通过电导测量不足以完全理解石墨烯量子点接触（QPCs）中各种复杂且相互竞争的传输机制。而散粒噪声（Shot noise）可以更深入地揭示电导测量无法观察到的微观模式分配。

Method: 该研究建立了一个混合框架，将紧束缚模拟与随机矩阵理论（RMT）相结合，用于预测散粒噪声和法诺因子。这些预测结果通过与实验测量的电导图进行验证。

Result: 研究发现，对于较高的朗道能级（NL > 0），系统表现出通用的混沌腔法诺因子 F ≈ 1/4。然而，对于零朗道能级（NL = 0），法诺因子收敛到一个特殊值 F = 1/3。这是因为零能级的亚晶格极化特性抑制了耦合，有效地将传输限制在单通道内。

Conclusion: 法诺因子（Fano factor）的差异（F=1/3 vs F=1/4）是区分石墨烯量子点接触中单通道与多通道混沌传输的直接噪声特征，而这是电导测量无法实现的。

Abstract: Graphene quantum point contacts (QPCs) in the quantum Hall regime host competing transport mechanisms including chiral edge propagation, valley degeneracy, and gate-induced mode mixing. Their interplay is not visible in conductance alone. Shot noise directly probes the statistics of transmission eigenvalues, revealing microscopic mode partitioning that conductance cannot access. We develop a hybrid framework combining tight-binding simulations of gate-defined graphene QPCs with random matrix theory (RMT) to predict shot noise and Fano factor signatures across different quantum Hall regimes, validated against experimental conductance maps of hBN-encapsulated graphene Hall bars. Three distinct regimes are identified: adiabatic propagation, sharp mode filtering, and multi-mode mixing driven by localized states beneath the split gate. For higher Landau levels ($N_L > 0$), complete mode mixing produces the universal chaotic-cavity limit $F \simeq 1/4$. Strikingly, the zeroth Landau level ($N_L = 0$) converges to $F = 1/3$. This distinct value originates in the sublattice polarization of the $N_L = 0$ edge state: coupling to mixed-sublattice localized states beneath the gate is suppressed, confining transport to an effective single channel ($N = 1$). Complete mixing within this single channel yields a flat transmission eigenvalue distribution and hence exactly $F = 1/3$ from single-channel RMT, numerically coincident with but mechanistically distinct from pseudo-diffusive zero-field graphene transport. The $F = 1/3$ versus $F = 1/4$ crossover is a Landau-level-resolved noise signature absent in conductance, providing a direct discriminator between single-channel and multi-channel chaotic transport in graphene QPCs.

</details>


### [31] [Supercurrent-Driven Néel Torque in Superconductor/Altermagnet Hybrids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22243)
*Hamed Vakili,Moaz Ali,Igor Žutić,Alexey A. Kovalev*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 这篇论文预测了在超导体/d波交替磁体异质结构中，超电流可以驱动尼尔自旋轨道力矩，从而实现对磁畴的无耗散控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探索一种无耗散控制尼尔矢量的方法，以应用于赛道内存、无耗散超导电子学和非传统计算等领域。

Method: 通过理论预测，研究了超导体/d波交替磁体异质结构。分析了由自旋轨道耦合和动量依赖的自旋分裂（在交替磁体中发现）相互作用产生的超电流驱动的尼尔自旋轨道力矩。

Result: 研究发现，超电流可以驱动尼尔自旋轨道力矩，该力矩与自旋三重态关联的出现有关。超电流的大小可以通过尼尔矢量的方向进行调节，并且这种力矩能够推动磁畴壁并反转畴壁内的尼尔矢量方向。

Conclusion: 研究结论是，超导体/交替磁体异质结构为实现尼尔矢量的无耗散控制提供了一个多功能平台，在未来技术中有巨大应用潜力。

Abstract: We predict a supercurrent-driven Néel spin-orbit torque in a superconductor/$d$-wave altermagnet heterostructure, associated with the emergence of spin-triplet correlations. The effect can be understood as a consequence of the supercurrent-induced spin polarization, owing to the interplay between spin-orbit coupling and momentum-dependent spin splitting, as found, for example, in altermagnets. Remarkably, the supercurrent can be tuned by the Néel-vector direction, and the supercurrent-induced torque can both propel magnetic domain walls and reverse the Néel-vector orientation within a domain wall. These findings establish superconductor/altermagnet heterostructures as a versatile platform for the dissipationless control of the Néel vector, with potential applications in racetrack memory, dissipationless superconducting electronics, and unconventional computing.

</details>

### [32] [Evolution of superconductivity from charge clusters to stripes in the $t$-$t'$-$J$ model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20368)
*Aritra Sinha,Hannes Karlsson,Martin Ulaga,Alexander Wietek*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过模拟发现，在铜基超导体中，超导配对首先在较高温度下局域于“空穴团簇”上，随着温度降低，这些局域的配对再扩展并连接起来，形成宏观的超导条纹相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在许多强关联电子体系（如铜基高温超导体）中，电荷序和超导电性之间的竞争与共存是一个核心特征，但它们之间的精确关系尚不明确。本文旨在阐明电荷涨落如何影响超导态，特别是在欠掺杂区域。

Method: 研究人员使用了有限温度张量网络模拟方法，对描述铜基超导体的$t$-$t'$-$J$模型进行了计算。他们通过模拟不同温度下的系统状态（热快照）来研究其物理特性。

Result: 在中等温度下，条纹融化形成空穴团簇，此时超导配对紧密地局域在这些团簇上。当温度降低进入条纹相时，配对开始在不同团簇之间退局域化，并最终在基态下形成贯穿整个系统的相干超导。这种“配对-电荷锁定”现象揭示了超导条纹相的母体状态。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了一个微观图像：欠掺杂铜基超导体中的超导起源于在磁关联驱动下形成的电荷团簇上的局域配对。这个图像与扫描隧道显微镜（STM）在临界温度以上观察到的局域配对，以及核磁共振（NMR）揭示的电荷团簇等实验现象相符，为理解超导与电荷序的关系提供了新的见解。

Abstract: Competition and coexistence of charge orders and superconductivity are hallmarks in many strongly correlated electron systems. Here, we unravel the precise role of charge fluctuations on the superconducting state in the $t$-$t'$-$J$ model of the high-temperature cuprate superconductors. Using finite-temperature tensor network simulations, we investigate thermal snapshots in the underdoped regime where the ground state features a superconducting stripe phase. At intermediate temperatures, where stripes have melted and hole clustering is observed, we find that pairing correlations are tightly localized on the hole clusters. Upon entering the stripe regime at lower temperatures, pairing increasingly delocalizes across different hole clusters to ultimately become coherent across the full system in the ground state. This pair-charge locking gives rise to an intuitive picture of the parent state of the superconducting stripe phase: pairing is localized on hole clusters formed via hole attraction due to the onset of magnetic correlations at intermediate temperature. We discuss how this microscopic picture is consistent with a broad range of experimental observations in cuprate superconductors, including scanning tunneling microscopy (STM) evidence for local pairing above $T_c$ and nuclear magnetic resonance (NMR) signatures of charge clustering in the underdoped regime.

</details>


### [33] [Collective Spin Excitations in Correlated Moiré Chern Ferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20370)
*Ming Xie,Sankar Das Sarma*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 这篇论文研究了TMD莫尔超晶格中的磁振子（自旋波）激发，发现其拓扑性质会显著影响磁序的稳定性和转变温度，尤其是在量子反常霍尔相中可以大幅提高该温度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在过渡金属二硫化物（TMD）的莫尔超晶格中，磁序是许多新奇量子态（如量子反常霍尔态）的母态。其稳定性受到低能集体自旋涨落（即磁振子）的关键影响，因此理解磁振子的性质至关重要。

Method: 该研究在整数填充因子 ν = -1 的条件下，理论上研究了磁振子激发的性质。通过调整层间位移场，作者计算并分析了磁振子能谱的拓扑特性及其能隙的变化。

Result: 研究发现，磁振子能谱的拓扑性质可通过调节层间位移场来改变。磁振子能隙的大小对基态的拓扑性质极为敏感，这导致在拓扑非平庸的量子反常霍尔相中，磁转变温度（Tc）比在拓扑平庸的关联绝缘体相中高出一个数量级。

Conclusion: 研究结果揭示了电子拓扑与磁振子拓扑之间的相互作用，为通过莫尔工程调控材料的磁性和拓扑性质提供了新的思路。

Abstract: Moiré-induced narrow electronic bands in transition metal dichalcogenide superlattices support many correlated quantum phases characterized by novel charge, flavor, and topological orders. Among these, magnetic ordering emerges as the most ubiquitous, often serving as the parent state for other correlated phases, including quantum anomalous Hall states, as well as chiral superconducting state. Because of electron-electron correlation, the stability of magnetic order is critically influenced by low-energy collective spin fluctuations, or magnon excitations. We investigate the nature of magnon excitations and their impact on the stability and transition temperature of the magnetic state at integer filling factor $ν= -1$. We find that the magnon spectrum exhibits isolated low-energy bands whose topological character undergoes a transition upon tuning the interlayer displacement field. The magnon gap is found to depend sensitively on the topology of the magnetic ground state, resulting in an order-of-magnitude enhancement of the transition temperature $T_c$ in the quantum anomalous Hall phase compared to the topologically trivial correlated insulator. Our findings provide insight into the interplay between electron and magnon topology and suggest new routes for controlling magnetism and topology via moiré engineering.

</details>


### [34] [Spin-reorientation as a switch for electronic topology in van der Waals ferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20457)
*Satyabrata Bera,Sudipta Chatterjee,Suman Kalyan Pradhan,Subhadip Pradhan,Arnab Bera,Sk Kalimuddin,Ashis K. Nandy,Mintu Mondal*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了二维范德华铁磁体 Fe4GeTe2 中的自旋重定向如何影响其拓扑电子结构和输运性质，发现该相变可以作为一种切换不同拓扑输运状态的内部开关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管自旋重定向转变（SRT）在二维金属铁磁体中很常见，但其对电子拓扑驱动的热力学和输运性质的影响在很大程度上仍是未知的。本研究旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 通过对室温准二维范德华铁磁体 Fe4GeTe2 (F4GT) 进行温度依赖的磁化强度、比热、磁输运和热电测量。

Result: 实验确认了在约 100K 附近存在磁易轴的重定向（SRT）。在该转变点附近，塞贝克系数、各向异性磁阻和霍尔效应均表现出明显异常，表明发生了费米面重构和能带拓扑结构的改变。反常霍尔电导率的分析表明，贝里曲率驱动的反常霍尔响应在 SRT 之上被强烈改变。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，自旋重定向可作为一种内部控制参数，用于在二维范德华铁磁体中切换不同的拓扑输运机制，为通过对称性控制来设计自旋极化电子态和功能提供了新途径。

Abstract: The interplay between spin reorientation and topological electronic structure in two-dimensional (2D) van der Waals (vdW) ferromagnets is central to understanding how magnetic anisotropy shapes charge transport. Although spin-reorientation transitions (SRTs) are common in 2D metallic ferromagnets, their impact on electronic-topology-driven thermodynamic and transport properties remains largely unexplored. Here we investigate this issue in Fe$_4$GeTe$_2$ (F4GT), a room-temperature quasi-2D vdW ferromagnet, using temperature-dependent magnetization, specific heat, magnetotransport, and thermoelectric measurements. Magnetization and specific heat establish a reorientation of the magnetic easy axis near $T_{\mathrm{SRT}} \sim 100$~K, in addition to ferromagnetic ordering at $T_C \sim 270$~K. Across the SRT, the Seebeck coefficient and anisotropic magnetoresistance show clear anomalies, indicating Fermi-surface reconstruction. The magnetoresistance exhibits a two-step field dependence: a low-field enhancement near the SRT associated with scattering from canted spins and evolving domains, followed by a higher-field negative response as spin fluctuations are suppressed. The simultaneous sign change of the ordinary Hall coefficient $R_0$ and the sharp anomaly in the anomalous Hall resistivity $ρ^{A}_{yx}$ further point to a temperature-driven modification of the underlying band topology. Analysis of the anomalous Hall conductivity $σ^{A}_{xy}$ and the scaling of $ρ^{A}_{yx}$ shows that the Berry-curvature-driven anomalous Hall response below $T_{\mathrm{SRT}}$ is strongly modified above the transition. Our results identify spin reorientation as an internal control parameter for switching between distinct topological transport regimes in a 2D vdW ferromagnet, providing a symmetry-controlled route to engineer spin-polarized electronic states and domain-texture-driven functionalities.

</details>


### [35] [Magnetic and electric properties of the metallic kagome antiferromagnet CrRhAs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20558)
*Franziska Breitner,Bin Shen,Anton Jesche,Alexander A. Tsirlin,Philipp Gegenwart*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 研究人员成功合成了 CrRhAs 单晶，并发现其在 150K 时会从顺磁性转变为反铁磁性。他们观察到该材料表现出奇特的霍尔效应行为，其信号的符号和大小与晶体方向和温度密切相关，这暗示了其内部存在复杂的电子结构和磁相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机源于理论预测：CrRhAs 是一种特殊的反铁磁 kagome 金属，可能拥有非平凡的自旋纹理。这激发了研究人员对其进行实验合成与物性探索的兴趣。

Method: 研究人员首先合成了 CrRhAs 单晶，随后通过电输运（电阻率、霍尔效应）、热容和磁化强度测量等实验手段，对其基本物理性质进行了表征。

Result: 实验结果确认 CrRhAs 在 150K 时发生反铁磁转变。霍尔效应测量显示，霍尔系数的符号会随着电流和磁场相对于晶体方向的改变而改变。此外，在进入反铁磁态后，霍尔系数会显著增强，暗示了费米面可能发生了重构。

Conclusion: 该研究结果表明 CrRhAs 具有与晶体结构方向相关的独特性质，其奇特的霍尔效应行为可能与费米面的特殊拓扑结构或马格农（magnon）散射有关。这些发现为探索奇异磁性系统中的反常电输运现象提供了实验指导。

Abstract: CrRhAs is an antiferromagnetic kagome metal predicted to host a nontrivial spin texture with vector spin chirality [Huang \textit{et al.}, \textit{npj Quantum Mater.} \textbf{8}, 32 (2023)]. We report the synthesis and basic characterization of CrRhAs single crystals, which exhibit an antiferromagnetic transition with $T_{\rm N}$ = 150~K, evidenced by electrical transport, heat capacity, and magnetization measurements. Hall resistivity varies linearly with magnetic field, i.e., there is no nonlinear Hall contribution. Intriguingly, the Hall coefficient changes sign between the configurations of $j \parallel ab, H \perp ab$ and $j \parallel c, H \perp c$, which is likely connected to a peculiar topology of the Fermi surface. Furthermore, for $j \parallel ab$, the Hall coefficient shows a pronounced and continuous enhancement below $T_{\rm N}$, signaling a significant reconstruction of the Fermi surface or an extra scattering from the magnons. Our results offer guidance for exploring anomalous electric transport phenomena in exotic magnetic systems.

### [36] [Unifying Variational and Dynamical Quantum Embedding: From Ghost Gutzwiller Approximation to Dynamical Mean-Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20559)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子嵌入（QE）理论中，动力学平均场理论（DMFT）和变分方法（如Gutzwiller近似）一直被看作是两种不同的范式。作者旨在将这两种观点联系起来，建立它们之间的桥梁。

Method: 论文通过数学证明，指出当辅助浴模（auxiliary bath modes）数量趋于无穷多时，一种名为“ghost-Gutzwiller 近似”（ghost-GA）的变分方法与动力学平均场理论（DMFT）变得完全等价。

Result: 这一理论统一带来了几个直接成果：1) 为 ghost-GA 方法提供了严格的有限温度扩展；2) 展示了如何仅通过静态期望值来计算物理格林函数，从而避免了传统方法中复杂的动力学计算；3) 证明了 ghost-GA、ghost-DMET 和 DMFT 是同一QE结构的不同表述。

Conclusion: 这项工作为未来发展超越DMFT的更高级理论提供了坚实的理论基础，并为研究强关联物质中的竞争相提供了新的计算途径。

Abstract: Dynamical and variational frameworks have long been viewed as distinct paradigms. In particular, in quantum embedding (QE) frameworks, dynamical mean-field theory (DMFT) captures nonperturbative dynamical correlations through a frequency-dependent self-energy, while the Gutzwiller approximation (GA) is formulated in terms of a variationally optimized ground-state wavefunction. Here we bridge these perspectives, proving that the ghost-Gutzwiller approximation (ghost-GA), which also admits a density-matrix-matching QE formulation known as ghost density matrix embedding theory (ghost-DMET), becomes strictly equivalent to DMFT in the limit of infinitely many auxiliary bath modes. This formal unification has immediate consequences. In particular, it yields a rigorous finite-temperature extension of ghost-GA and shows that the physical Green's function can be determined from static expectation values of the embedding Hamiltonians, providing a route to computational studies of competing phases in strongly correlated matter with DMFT-level accuracy, while bypassing the need to calculate dynamical spectra with conventional impurity solvers. More broadly, it shows that the variational ghost-GA, the density-matrix-matching ghost-DMET formulation, and the dynamical DMFT description are not separate constructions, but complementary formulations of the same QE structure, thereby providing a concrete formal basis for future controlled extensions beyond DMFT.

### [43] [Tangent equations of motion for nonlinear response functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22137)
*Atsushi Ono*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为切线运动方程（TEOM）的新方法，可以直接从实时动力学中高效计算高阶非线性响应函数，避免了传统方法的组合爆炸和数值不稳定性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算高阶非线性响应函数在计算上成本极高，因为存在组合（通常是阶乘）扩展或严重的数值误差问题，这限制了对其的评估。

Method: 作者建立了一个基于函数空间中关于外场的加托导数（Gateaux derivative）的切线运动方程（TEOM）框架。通过将TEOM与原始动力学方程一起演化，可以高精度地分离出每个微扰阶数，从而逐项分解物理贡献。

Result: 该方法成功计算了固态电子模型的五阶频率分辨响应函数，并以可控的精度获得了经典杜芬振子（Duffing oscillator）高达49阶的非线性响应函数。此外，该方法能够直接且稳定地计算光学电导率，即使在零频率附近也是如此。

Conclusion: TEOM框架具有通用性，可以无缝集成到现有的实时演化方法中，为计算量子和经典动力学系统中的非线性响应函数提供了一个通用的解决方案。

Abstract: Nonlinear response functions, formulated as multipoint correlation functions or Volterra kernels, encode the dynamical and spectroscopic properties of physical systems and underpin a wide range of nonlinear transport and optical phenomena. However, their evaluation rapidly becomes prohibitive at high orders because of combinatorial (often factorial) scaling or severe numerical errors. Here, we establish a systematic and efficient framework to compute nonlinear response functions directly from real-time dynamics, without explicitly constructing multipoint correlators or relying on numerically unstable finite-difference methods for order-resolved extraction. Our approach is based on the Gateaux derivative with respect to the external field in function space, which yields a closed hierarchy of tangent equations of motion (TEOM). Propagating the TEOM alongside the original dynamics isolates each perturbative order with high accuracy, providing a term-by-term decomposition of physical contributions. The computational cost scales exponentially with response order in the fully general setting and reduces to polynomial complexity when all perturbation directions are identical; both regimes avoid the factorial scaling of explicit multipoint-correlator evaluations. We demonstrate the power of TEOM by computing frequency-resolved fifth-order response functions for a solid-state electron model and by obtaining nonlinear response functions up to the 49th order with controlled accuracy in a classical Duffing oscillator. We further show that our time-evolution formulation allows optical conductivities to be evaluated directly while remaining numerically stable even near zero frequency. TEOM can be incorporated seamlessly into existing real-time evolution methods, yielding a general framework for computing nonlinear response functions in quantum and classical dynamical systems.

### [44] [Green parafermions as emergent flat-band excitations in condensed matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21238)
*Huan-Qiang Zhou,Ian P. McCulloch,Murray T. Batchelor*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究发现，长期以来被认为是纯数学概念的“绿色准费米子”（Green parafermions），实际上可以在经历特定类型对称性破缺的凝聚态物质系统中作为复合激发涌现出来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 绿色准费米子（Green parafermions）在理论上已被提出很久，但通常被认为只是一种缺乏物理实现的数学概念。本研究旨在证明这类准粒子可以在真实的凝聚态物理系统中出现。

Method: 研究人员通过在由部分平移对称性破缺产生的演生晶胞上引入辅助马约拉纳费米子。将这些辅助粒子视为物理自由度或虚拟自由度，从而构建出绿色准费米子态。

Result: 研究发现，当辅助马约拉纳费米子被视为物理自由度时，所产生的绿色准费米子态对应于满足三线性代数的平带激发。而当其被视为虚拟时，该构造解释了指数级简并基态的出现，并揭示了绿色准费米子与黄金螺旋等自相似几何对象之间的惊人对应关系。

Conclusion: 该论文得出结论，具有B类戈德斯通模式的凝聚态系统为绿色准费米子提供了一个自然的物理环境，使其可以作为一种新兴的、可能被观测到的准粒子存在。这一结论在铁磁性自旋-1双二次模型和铁磁性SU(2)平带Tasaki模型中得到了具体验证。

Abstract: Green parafermions, originally introduced by Green and extended by Greenberg and Messiah through trilinear and relative trilinear commutation relations beyond Bose-Fermi statistics, are generally regarded as mathematical curiosities without physical realization. We show that these paraparticles can in fact emerge as composite excitations in a broad class of condensed-matter systems undergoing spontaneous symmetry breaking with type-B Goldstone modes. The key ingredient is the introduction of auxiliary Majorana fermions defined on emergent unit cells produced by partial translational-symmetry breaking. When the auxiliary Majoranas are treated as physical degrees of freedom, the resulting Green parafermion states (up to a projection operator) correspond to flat-band excitations, whose creation and annihilation operators satisfy the trilinear algebra. When they are regarded as fictitious, the same construction explains the appearance of exponentially many degenerate ground states and reveals a surprising correspondence between Green parafermions and self-similar geometric objects, such as the golden spiral. Explicit realizations are demonstrated for the ferromagnetic spin-1 biquadratic model and the ferromagnetic $\rm {SU}(2)$ flat-band Tasaki model, showing that condensed-matter systems with type-B Goldstone modes provide a natural setting for Green parafermions as emergent, possibly observable quasiparticles.

</details>


### [45] [Symmetry group factorization and unitary equivalence among Temperley-Lieb integrable models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21242)
*Huan-Qiang Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文揭示了两种Temperley-Lieb (TL)可积模型——q态量子Potts (QP)模型和交错SU(n)自旋链——之间隐藏的联系。研究表明，在特定条件下，它们是酉等价的，这意味着这些看似不同的模型本质上是相同物理系统的不同表现形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究并揭示两种被广泛研究的Temperley-Lieb (TL)可积模型序列，即q态量子Potts (QP)模型和交错SU(n)自旋链之间的“隐藏联系”。

Method: 论文通过建立“酉等价”关系来证明其结论。首先，它展示了对称群的分解特性：当参数q或n可以分解为两个数的乘积时，模型可以酉等价地变换为一个组合模型。其次，它建立了交错SU(n)自旋链与q态QP模型之间的直接酉等价关系，其中q=n²，但这需要将自旋链的尺寸加倍，并翻转铁磁/反铁磁类型。

Result: 论文证明了q态QP模型和交错SU(n)自旋链中都存在对称群分解现象。更重要的是，它证明了铁磁（FM）的交错SU(n)自旋链酉等价于反铁磁（AF）的q态QP模型（其中q=n²），反之亦然，前提是链的尺寸需加倍。这些等价关系揭示了一族本质上相同但表现形式不同的模型。

Conclusion: 不同的Temperley-Lieb可积模型在本质上并非根本不同，而是可以被视为同一物理系统的不同“伪装”。该研究阐明了这些不同TL可积模型之间酉等价性的物理意义。

Abstract: It is shown that there is a hidden connection between the two well-studied sequences of the Temperley-Lieb (TL) integrable models -- the $q$-state quantum Potts (QP) models at the self-dual points and the staggered ${\rm SU}(n)$ spin-$s$ chains with $n=2s+1$ ($s \ge 1$), in addition to the uniform ${\rm SU}(2)$ spin-$1/2$ Heisenberg model. For each sequence, symmetry group factorization arises, in the sense that if $q$ is factorized into $q_1$ and $q_2$, then the $q$-state QP model is unitarily equivalent to a combined QP model with the symmetry group ${\rm S}_{q_1} \times {\rm S}_{q_2}$ or if $n$ is factorized into $n_1$ and $n_2$, then the staggered ${\rm SU}(n)$ spin-$s$ chain with the symmetry group ${\rm SU}(n)$ is unitarily equivalent to a combined staggered ${\rm SU}(n_1) \times {\rm SU}(n_2)$ spin chain with the symmetry group ${\rm SU}(n_1) \times {\rm SU}(n_2)$, valid for both ferromagnetic (FM) and antiferromagnetic (AF) cases. Moreover, the FM (AF) staggered ${\rm SU}(n)$ spin-$s$ chain is unitarily equivalent to the AF (FM) $q$-state QP model with $q=n^2$, as long as the size of the AF (FM) staggered ${\rm SU}(n)$ spin-$s$ chain is doubled. A combination of the two distinct types of unitary equivalences yields a family of models such that they are essentially identical, but appear in different guises. Some physical implications for unitary equivalence among different TL integrable models are clarified.

### [46] [Non-invertible symmetries and boundary conditions for the transverse-field Ising model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21290)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在为自对偶的横场伊辛模型（TFIM）在各种边界条件下（特别是那些破坏平移不变性的情况）构建非互换的KW对偶对称性，并希望确保该构造在热力学极限下是自洽的，同时与现有理论进行比较。

Method: 通过引入额外的自由度来“扩展”希尔伯特空间。这个技巧可以将原始空间中非平移不变的哈密顿量，转化为扩展空间中平移不变的哈密顿量，从而方便地构建非互换的Kramers-Wannier (KW)对偶对称性，并推导其融合规则。

Result: 研究成功构建了KW对偶对称性，并发现其融合规则类似于Tambara-Yamagami Z2融合范畴。对于周期性和反周期性边界条件，其结果与先前工作一致；但对于对偶扭曲的边界条件，研究结果与先前工作存在差异。

Conclusion: 该论文提出的构造方法是有效的，并确保了物理结果在热力学极限下的一致性。该研究不仅复现了部分已知结果，还揭示了在对偶扭曲边界条件下与现有理论的潜在差异，指出了未来值得进一步研究的方向。

Abstract: Non-invertible Kramers-Wannier (KW) duality symmetries are constructed for the transverse-field Ising model (TFIM) at the self-dual point under various boundary conditions (BCs), as long as the resultant Hamiltonian commutes with the ${\rm Z}_2$ symmetry operator. This is achieved by introducing extra degrees of freedom into the Hilbert space, in order to turn a non-translation-invariant Hamiltonian in the original Hilbert space into a translation-invariant Hamiltonian in the augmented Hilbert space. One may lift the trivial identity operator, the ${\rm Z}_2$ symmetry operator and the non-invertible KW duality symmetry operator to their counterparts in the augmented Hilbert space, valid for each of four types of toroidal BCs. As it turns out, they yield a lattice version of fusion rules, which bears a resemblance to the Tambara-Yamagami ${\rm Z}_2$ fusion category. Our construction is thus consistent with the basic physical requirement that all possible BCs should yield a converging result in the thermodynamic limit. In particular, the lattice versions of fusion rules, constructed by Seiberg, Seifnashri and Shao [SciPost Phys. \textbf{16}, 154 (2024)], are reproduced for periodic and anti-periodic BCs, but a discrepancy is revealed for duality-twisted BCs.

Abstract: Magnetic polarons can generate colossal magnetoresistance in magnetic semiconductors, yet their terahertz electrodynamics remain largely unexplored. These results demonstrate that magnetic polarons strongly govern the low-energy electrodynamics and highlight the sensitivity of terahertz spectroscopy to polaronic magnetotransport in correlated magnetic semiconductors.

Abstract: The temperature and strain dependences of the optical conductivity spectrum of hexagonal manganese telluride (MnTe) were measured, revealing absorption in the terahertz (THz) region from spin-split bands to acceptor levels. The temperature dependence was attributed to a change in the altermagnetic electronic structure. A Fano-like antisymmetric line shape in the optical phonon absorption was observed, which originates from the interaction between optical phonons and the spin-split bands. Additionally, under negative uniaxial pressure, the THz peak shifts away from the Fermi level (EF), suggesting that spin-splitting bands at energies away from EF, consistent with the theoretical prediction that the spin-splitting angle decreases. The observed behavior of the THz peak clearly shows that MnTe has the altermagnetic electronic structure.

### [50] [Dynamical spin correlations in kagome antiferromagnets: comparison of Abrikosov fermion and Schwinger boson approaches beyond mean field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21513)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kagome晶格反铁磁体是量子自旋液体的有力候选者，但其激发谱的性质（如是否存在自旋能隙和规范结构）仍存在争议。以往的研究分别使用阿布里科索夫费米子和施温格玻色子这两种方法，但缺乏直接比较，因此不清楚这两种理论框架在描述自旋动力学和规范结构方面的异同。

Result: 研究发现，阿布里科索夫费米子理论得到的动态自旋结构因子呈现圆顶状特征，且其连续谱结构严重依赖于规范结构的选择。而施温格玻色子理论则在低能区给出了不同的凹形结构。当在施温格玻色子理论中引入多体效应后，模型的低能能隙显著减小，低能谱权重增强，这与实验观测结果非常吻合。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，在施温格玻色子理论中考虑多体效应对于准确描述kagome晶格反铁磁体的低能自旋动力学至关重要。该方法在与实验观测进行比较时，似乎比阿布里科索夫费米子方法更具优势。

Abstract: Quantum spin liquids exhibit fractionalized spin excitations as a consequence of strong quantum many-body effects. The kagome antiferromagnetic Heisenberg model is a promising candidate for a quantum spin-liquid ground state; however, the nature of its excitation spectrum remains controversial, particularly regarding the presence of a spin gap and the gauge structure coupled to fractional quasiparticles. To address these issues, parton approaches have been extensively employed, where spin operators are represented in terms of fermionic or bosonic quasiparticles within the Abrikosov fermion and Schwinger boson frameworks. Thus far, these approaches have been pursued independently, and it has remained unclear how the results obtained from these frameworks compare, particularly with respect to the spin dynamics and gauge structure of the kagome antiferromagnet. Here, we investigate the dynamical spin structure factor of the antiferromagnetic Heisenberg model with a Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction on the kagome lattice, relevant to herbertsmithite, by employing both approaches. We find that the dynamical spin structure factor obtained from the Abrikosov fermion mean-field theory exhibits dome-shaped features, and that its continuum structure significantly depends on the gauge structure of the spin-liquid ansatz. On the other hand, the Schwinger boson mean-field theory yields a concave-down structure in the low-energy region, distinct from that obtained using the Abrikosov fermion approach. Moreover, incorporating many-body effects beyond the mean-field approximation substantially reduces the low-energy gap and enhances the low-energy spectral weight, consistent with experimental observations. Our results suggest the importance of many-body effects in the Schwinger boson theory for capturing the low-energy spin dynamics of kagome antiferromagnets.

  <summary>Details</summary>

### [53] [Drinfeld Center as Quantum State Monodromy over Bloch Hamiltonians around Defects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22029)
*Hisham Sati,Urs Schreiber*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文展示了Drinfeld中心融合范畴 Z(Vec_G) 如何描述分数拓扑绝缘体材料中布里渊区点缺陷附近的拓扑序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Drinfeld中心融合范畴 Z(Vec_G) 以其在某些晶格模型中模拟任意子而闻名。作者旨在探究其融合规则是否也能描述分数拓扑绝缘体材料中的拓扑序，特别是在布里渊区的点缺陷附近。

Method: 作者通过数学证明来建立联系。他们证明了 Z(Vec_G) 在布里渊区的一个穿孔盘上，局部地反映了带隙量子态的单值性（拓扑序）。这些量子态是基于布洛赫哈密顿量的参数空间构建的，而该参数空间的分类空间的基本群为G。

Result: 研究证明了 Z(Vec_G) 确实能够局部反映在特定参数空间下的带隙量子态的单值性，即拓扑序。

Conclusion: 该研究成功地将Drinfeld中心融合范畴 Z(Vec_G) 的应用从晶格模型中的任意子扩展到了分数拓扑绝缘体材料。这为理解这些材料在布里渊区点缺陷附近的拓扑序提供了一个新的数学工具和视角。

Abstract: The Drinfeld center fusion category $\mathcal{Z}(\mathrm{Vec}_G)$ famously models anyons in certain lattice models. Here we demonstrate how its fusion rules may also describe topological order in fractional topological insulator materials, in the vicinity of point defects in the Brillouin zone.
  Concretely, we prove that $\mathcal{Z}(\mathrm{Vec}_G)$ reflects, locally over a punctured disk in the Brillouin zone, the monodromy (topological order) of gapped quantum states over the parameter space of Bloch Hamiltonians whose classifying space has fundamental group $G$.

</details>


### [54] [An Exact Conjugation Identity for the Many-Body Wilson-Loop Beyond Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22217)
*Kai Watanabe*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文为多体系统的威尔逊循环（Wilson-loop）建立了一个精确的共轭恒等式 $W(-\delta)=W(\delta)^*$，此恒等式在贝里相位未被对称性量化的情况下依然成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究多体系统中的威尔逊循环 $W(\delta)$ 在特定对称变换下的性质，特别是在键二聚化参数 $\delta$ 和磁通量参数 $\theta$ 反向时，从而得出一个超越对称性保护体系的普适关系。

Method: 1. 理论上，通过寻找一个组合反幺正映射，证明了威尔逊循环共轭恒等式 $W(-\delta)=W(\delta)^*$ 的存在。
2. 以半填充的二聚化交错哈伯德环（dimerized staggered Hubbard ring）为具体模型进行微观构建。
3. 使用密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）方法对该恒等式进行了数值验证。

Result: 1. 证实了恒等式 $W(-\delta)=W(\delta)^*$ 的成立。
2. 推论出贝里相位满足 $\gamma(-\delta) = -\gamma(\delta) \pmod{2\pi}$。
3. 关键在于，此恒等式在贝里相位不被对称性量化为0或$\pi$的有能隙区域依然有效。
4. 该关系可推广到更一般的格点模型。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一个关于多体威尔逊循环的精确共轭恒等式，其成立条件是一个组合反幺正对称性。这个恒等式为多体系统中的几何相位（贝里相位）提供了一个普遍的约束，其适用范围超越了贝里相位被对称性量化的体系。

Abstract: We establish an exact Wilson-loop conjugation identity, $W(-δ)=W(δ)^*$, for the many-body overlap Wilson-loop $W(δ)$ accumulated along a $U(1)$ flux-threading (twist) cycle parametrized by $θ\in[0,2π]$, where $δ$ denotes the bond-dimerization parameter. A minimal sufficient condition is the existence of a composite antiunitary mapping acting on the flux-threaded Hamiltonian family that implements $(δ,θ)\mapsto(-δ,-θ)$. As a concrete demonstration, we construct such a mapping microscopically in a dimerized staggered Hubbard ring at half filling. We then verify the conjugation identity using the density-matrix renormalization group (DMRG) for gapped, nondegenerate ground states along the twist cycle. Importantly, the identity persists in depinned gapped regimes where the Berry-phase $γ\equiv-\arg W$ is not symmetry-quantized; as a corollary, $γ(-δ)=-γ(δ)$ (mod $2π$). More generally, the same conjugation relation applies to any lattice model whose flux-threaded Hamiltonian family is closed under an orientation reversal of the bond pattern (a suitable permutation of link-hopping parameters) combined with a reversal of the flux orientation.

</details>


### [55] [Emergent relativistic symmetry from interacting fermions on the honeycomb bilayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22259)
*Zi Hong Liu,Lukas Janssen*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文使用量子蒙特卡罗方法研究了蜂窝双层晶格上无自旋费米子的相互作用，发现了一个从狄拉克半金属到绝缘体的量子相变，该相变属于 Gross-Neveu-Ising 普适类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机是理解在电中性的蜂窝双层结构中，相互作用如何影响具有二次色散的无自旋费米子系统。在无相互作用时，该系统在布里渊区的角上具有特殊的能带接触点，加入相互作用后的行为是理论研究的重点。

Method: 研究人员使用了大规模量子蒙特卡罗（Quantum Monte Carlo）模拟来研究该系统的相图。

Result: 1. 在弱到中等相互作用下，二次能带接触点分裂成四个狄拉克点。 2. 强相互作用导致形成层极化的电荷密度波，从而转变为绝缘态。 3. 从半金属到绝缘体的量子相变是连续的，其临界指数与 (2+1) 维 Gross-Neveu-Ising 普适类的理论预测值在 5% 的偏差内相符。 4. 确定了不同温度和相互作用强度下的相变和交叉尺度。

Conclusion: 该研究成功揭示了蜂窝双层费米子系统的相图，并证明了其量子相变属于 Gross-Neveu-Ising 普适类。这一发现为该量子临界现象提供了一个具体的物理实现，并通过精确的临界指数计算验证了理论预测。

Abstract: We study the phase diagram of interacting spinless fermions on the honeycomb bilayer at charge neutrality using large-scale quantum Monte Carlo simulations. In the noninteracting limit, the low-energy spectrum features quadratically dispersing bands that touch at the corners of the hexagonal Brillouin zone. Weak to intermediate interactions induce a splitting of each of the quadratic band touching points into four Dirac points, located along high-symmetry directions of the reciprocal lattice. Strong interactions lead to the formation of a layer-polarized charge density wave, which spontaneously breaks the $\mathbb Z_2$ layer inversion symmetry and opens an insulating gap in the spectrum. We show that the semimetal-to-insulator quantum phase transition as a function of interaction is continuous and characterized by emergent relativistic symmetry. Our results for the values of the correlation-length exponent $ν$, the order-parameter anomalous dimension $η_φ$, and the fermion anomalous dimension $η_ψ$ agree with those of the theoretically predicted 2+1D Gross-Neveu-Ising universality class with eight two-component Dirac fermions within less than 5\%\ deviation. We also determine the crossover scale as a function of interaction strength between the nonrelativistic semimetal state at high temperatures, characterized by dynamical critical exponent $z = 2$, and the Dirac semimetal state at intermediates temperatures, characterized by $z=1$. Further reducing the temperature below the crossover scale at a fixed value of the interaction strength above the quantum critical point results in a classical ordering transition in the 2D Ising universality class.

</details>

### [56] [Probabilistic calibration of crystal plasticity material models with synthetic global and local data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20241)
*Joshua D. Pribe,Patrick E. Leser,Saikumar R. Yeratapally,George Weber*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于晶体塑性模型的两阶段贝叶斯校准程序，该程序结合了全局和局部数据，并使用替代模型和全场模拟来有效量化参数不确定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 仅使用全局数据校准晶体塑性模型会导致参数不唯一；而使用局部数据（如HEDM实验）虽然可以解决此问题，但成本高昂且计算量巨大，难以进行不确定性量化。

Method: 该研究提出了一种两阶段校准程序。首先结合替代模型和顺序蒙特卡洛算法，使用全局（应力-应变曲线）和局部（晶粒平均应力）合成数据进行贝叶斯推断。然后通过全场晶体塑性模拟进行微调，以实现高效且准确的参数校准和不确定性量化。

Result: 实验结果表明，该两阶段程序计算效率高。加入局部数据能显著减少参数的不确定性，即使在局部数据有限且有噪声的情况下，该程序依然稳健。此外，校准参数的联合分布揭示了模型参数之间的相关性。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了所提出的两阶段校准程序在计算上是高效的，并且局部数据对于减少参数不确定性至关重要。这种结合全局和局部数据的方法为晶体塑性模型的精确校准和不确定性分析提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Crystal plasticity models connect macroscopic deformation with the physics of microscale slip in polycrystalline materials. These models can be calibrated using global stress-strain curves, but the resulting parametrization is often not unique: multiple parametrizations can predict the same global behavior but different local, grain-scale behavior. Using local data for calibration can mitigate uniqueness issues, but expensive specialized experiments like high-energy X-ray diffraction (HEDM) are typically required to gather the data. The computational expense of full-field simulations also often prevents uncertainty quantification with sampling-based calibration algorithms like Markov chain Monte Carlo. This study presents a two-stage calibration procedure that combines global and local data and balances the efficiency of a surrogate model with the accuracy of full-field crystal plasticity simulations. The procedure quantifies uncertainty using Bayesian inference with an efficient, parallelized sequential Monte Carlo algorithm. Calibrations are completed using synthetic data with a microstructure representative of Inconel 718 to assess uncertainty and accuracy of the parameters relative to a known ground truth. Global data comes from the uniaxial stress-strain curve, while local data comes from grain-average stresses, reflecting typical outputs of HEDM experiments. Additional calibrations with limited and noisy local data demonstrate robustness of the procedure and identify the most important features of the data. Overall, the results demonstrate the computational efficiency of the two-stage procedure and the value of local data for reducing parameter uncertainty. In addition, joint distributions of the calibrated parameters highlight key considerations in choosing constitutive models and calibration data, including challenges resulting from correlated parameters.

</details>


### [57] [A chemical language model for reticular materials design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20389)
*Dhruv Menon,Vivek Singh,Xu Chen,Mohammad Reza Alizadeh Kiapi,Ivan Zyuzin,Hamish W. Macleod,Nakul Rampal,William Shepard,Omar M. Yaghi,David Fairen-Jimenez*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一个名为 Nexerra-R1 的化学语言模型，它可以通过逆向设计，智能地生成用于构建金属有机框架（MOF）的有机连接体，从而高效地发现具有特定功能的新材料，并成功合成了完全由计算机设计的全新材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，新的金属有机框架（MOF）的发现主要依赖于研究者的直觉和反复实验，这种方法效率低下，并且只能探索巨大化学空间中的一小部分。因此，需要一种更系统、更高效的方法来发现具有特定性能的材料。

Method: 研究者开发了一个名为 Nexerra-R1 的构建块化学语言模型。该模型不直接生成完整的 MOF 结构，而是在分子构建块的层面上操作，生成有机的“连接体”（linker）。它结合了流引导分布靶向技术来引导生成过程，以满足特定应用目标，然后将生成的连接体在计算机中组装成三维框架并进行结构优化。

Result: 该模型策略的有效性得到了验证，它不仅成功地“重新发现”了一些已知的 MOF 材料，还完全通过计算机设计，并成功地在实验中合成了一种前所未有的新框架材料 CU-525。

Conclusion: 该研究为网状化学材料建立了一个通用的逆向设计范式，通过可控的化学语言模型，实现了从计算设计到可合成新材料的直接转化。

Abstract: Reticular chemistry has enabled the synthesis of tens of thousands of metal-organic frameworks (MOFs), yet the discovery of new materials still relies largely on intuition-driven linker design and iterative experimentation. As a result, researchers explore only a small fraction of the vast chemical space accessible to reticular materials, limiting the systematic discovery of frameworks with targeted properties. Here, we introduce Nexerra-R1, a building-block chemical language model that enables inverse design in reticular chemistry through the targeted generation of organic linkers. Rather than generating complete frameworks directly, Nexerra-R1 operates at the level of molecular building blocks, preserving the modular logic that underpins reticular synthesis. The model supports both unconstrained generation of low-connectivity linkers and scaffold-constrained design of symmetric multidentate motifs compatible with predefined nodes and topologies. We further combine linker generation with flow-guided distributional targeting to steer the generative process toward application-relevant objectives while maintaining chemical validity and assembly feasibility. The generated linkers are subsequently assembled into three-dimensional frameworks and are structurally optimized to produce candidate materials compatible with experimental synthesis. Using Nexerra-R1, we validate this strategy by rediscovering known MOFs and by proposing the experimental synthesis of a previously unreported framework, CU-525, generated entirely in silico. Together, these results establish a general inverse-design paradigm for reticular materials in which controllable chemical language modelling enables the direct translation from computational design to synthesizable frameworks.

</details>

*Boyang Zhao,Youngjun Ahn,Qinwen Deng,Yidai Liu,Sijie Xu,Donald A. Walko,Stephan O. Hruszkewycz,Pengcheng Dai,Liang Wu,Haidan Wen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究关联电子材料中电荷、自旋与晶格自由度之间的相互作用，特别是澄清kagome金属FeGe中电荷密度波（CDW）与晶格畸变之间的关系。

Method: 使用高分辨率X射线衍射进行温度依赖性测量，并结合朗道自由能分析。

Result: 在CDW相变温度下，观测到晶格反射峰分裂，这直接证明了该相变为一级结构相变。研究还发现，长程CDW序只存在于面外晶格常数被压缩的结构中，且强晶格-电荷耦合是稳定CDW序的关键。

Abstract: The intertwining of charge, spin, and lattice degrees of freedom underlies the emergent properties of correlated materials. A recent prominent example is the kagome metal FeGe, which hosts coexisting charge density wave (CDW) and antiferromagnetic orders, accompanied by a lattice distortion associated with partial Ge-Ge dimerization. Using temperature-dependent high-resolution X-ray diffraction measurements, we observed a robust splitting of the lattice reflection into two coexisting peaks with distinct lattice constants at the CDW transition temperature TCDW, providing direct evidence for a first-order structural phase transition that is absent in samples with suppressed CDW order. Furthermore, the long-range CDW order was found to be only commensurate with lattice structures with the compressed out-of-plane lattice constant. The Landau free energy analysis shows that strong lattice-charge coupling is a key factor in stabilizing long-range CDW order. Our work clarifies the critical role of structural transformation in the CDW formation and opens opportunities for strain control of electronic phases in FeGe.

### [59] [Composition dependence of the critical Rayleigh number curve for macrosegregation in multicomponent metal alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20569)
*Owain S. Houghton,Adrian S. Sabau,Gregory B. Olson*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过扩展Flemings模型，推导了新的瑞利数（Ra）判据来预测半固态糊状区中由局部重熔引起的通道缺陷形成。研究发现，临界瑞利数（Racrit）受固相分数和热物理性质影响，因此具有很强的成分依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在半固态糊状区中的对流不稳定性会导致形成通道，从而引发雀斑、通道偏析和A型偏析等缺陷。为了更好地预测和控制这些缺陷的产生，需要确定这些不稳定性（特别是局部重熔）开始的条件。

Method: 本文扩展了Flemings模型，推导了用于判断局部重熔是否发生的瑞利数（Ra）及其临界值（Racrit）的表达式。研究人员利用CALPHAD提供的热物理数据，并结合镍基高温合金SX-1和铅锡合金的实验与数值研究结果，对这些表达式进行了评估。同时，还针对多种钢的成分，测试了此判据与现有经验判据的关联性。

Result: 研究发现，临界瑞利数（Racrit）并非一个恒定值，它会随着局部平均固相分数和多种热物理性质的变化而变化。

Conclusion: 由于材料的热物理性质在很小的成分范围内就可能发生显著变化，研究得出结论，临界瑞利数（Racrit）是一个强烈依赖于材料成分的参数。这意味着预测缺陷形成需要精确考虑具体合金的成分。

Abstract: Convective instabilities in the semi-solid mushy zone can trigger channel formation that leads to defects known as freckles, channel segregates and A-type segregates. In the present work, Flemings' model is extended to determine conditions for the onset of local remelting in an initially stagnant mushy zone. Expressions for the Rayleigh number $Ra$ and its critical value $Ra_{\rm crit}$, above which channels may form due to local remelting, are derived. Using thermophysical data from CALPHAD, these expressions are evaluated using results from benchmark experimental and numerical studies for the nickel-based superalloy SX-1 and Pb-Sn alloys. The correlation of this $Ra$-based criterion with previously reported empirical criteria is also tested for various steel compositions. It is found that $Ra_{\rm crit}$ varies with the local average solid fraction and several thermophysical properties. Since these properties can vary substantially within a relatively narrow composition range, it is suggested that $Ra_{\rm crit}$ is a strongly composition dependent parameter.
