Conclusion: 该研究成功地进行了一次受控的软QCD重调谐，新模型在广泛的观测数据上提升了模拟精度，同时明确了其局限性，为高能物理实验提供了更可靠的模拟工具。

Abstract: We present a sequential nine-parameter retune of PYTHIA 8.316, built on the Monash 2013 baseline, for soft-QCD observables in proton--proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}=0.9$--$13$ TeV. The tune is constructed with direct generator evaluation and developed in stages: an initial five-parameter localization in the hadronization-sensitive sector, successive extensions driven by multi-energy minimum-bias tensions, and a final expansion to a broader soft-QCD fit basis. The fitted set includes minimum-bias charged-particle data, identified-hadron spectra and ratios, underlying-event observables, and event-shape distributions. A separate held-out validation basis is kept outside the fit.
  The final tune retunes nine non-perturbative parameters controlling fragmentation, strangeness suppression, diquark production, color reconnection, MPI regularization and its energy dependence, the impact-parameter overlap profile, and transverse-momentum generation in string breaking. On the common fit basis, the grouped score density improves from $99.18$ for Monash 2013 to $85.67$. The strongest gains occur in the 13 TeV minimum-bias and underlying-event sectors, with further improvement in the ALICE identified-hadron blocks and a smaller gain in the CMS 13 TeV identified-hadron sector. Monash remains better in the CMS 7 TeV underlying-event block and the ATLAS 7 TeV event-shape block, while the low-energy charged-particle sector remains the main unresolved tension for both tunes.
  The held-out validation basis supports the same picture. Monash remains slightly better in the low-energy CMS validation blocks, but the present tune performs better in the ATLAS early underlying-event block and in both held-out 13 TeV charged-particle sectors. We interpret it as a controlled soft-QCD retune that improves a broad set of observables while keeping its limitations explicit.

### [115] [CP-violation and its implications in a complex singlet extension of 2HDM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21483)
*Jayita Lahiri,Gudrid Moortgat-Pick*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了在双希格斯二重模型（2HDM）的复单态扩展中的CP破坏现象，探讨了该模型在满足电偶极矩（EDM）和暗物质约束下的参数空间，并分析了在未来对撞机上探测CP破坏信号的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型中的CP破坏不足以解释宇宙的物质-反物质不对称性。因此，本文旨在探索标准模型之外的新CP破坏来源。具体而言，研究通用双希格斯二重模型（2HDM）的复单态扩展，因为它提供了一个额外的CP破坏来源，有潜力在满足严格的电偶极矩（EDM）等实验约束的同时，解释CP破坏现象。

Method: 1. 在通用双希格斯二重模型（2HDM）的复单态扩展框架下进行理论分析。 2. 首先，在125 GeV希格斯玻色子与标准模型（SM）完全一致的假设下，识别出模型中新的CP破坏来源。 3. 将暗物质纳入模型，并分析其相关约束对模型参数空间和CP破坏相位的影响。 4. 探索在未来对撞机上通过非标准标量粒子之间的CP破坏三线性耦合来探测这种情景的可能性。 5. 最后，偏离精确对齐极限，研究观测到的希格斯玻色子的CP性质。

Result: 1. 该模型相比于2HDM，提供了一个额外的CP破坏来源，使其能更容易地满足严格的电偶极矩（EDM）约束。 2. 暗物质领域的约束会影响模型的参数空间及与CP破坏相位的相互作用。 3. 在未来的对撞机实验中，有可能通过非标准标量粒子间CP破坏的三线性耦合来探测到相关信号。 4. 希格斯玻色子CP相位的探测前景具有很强的模型依赖性，这体现在费米子耦合和希格斯玻色子的三线性自耦合中。

Conclusion: 本文论证了通用双希格斯二重模型（2HDM）的复单态扩展是研究CP破坏的一个有前景的框架。该模型不仅提供了一个新的CP破坏来源，缓解了与电偶极矩（EDM）约束的紧张关系，还展示了与暗物质现象的潜在联系。未来的对撞机实验，特别是通过对希格斯玻色子性质的精确测量，有望为验证或排除该模型提供关键证据，尽管探测前景具有显著的模型依赖性。

Abstract: We investigate CP-violation in the complex singlet extension of the general Two Higgs Doublet Model (2HDM) with Yukawa alignment condition. We first explore the possibility of explicit CP-violation in the extended scalar sector while the 125 GeV Higgs remains exactly Standard Model (SM)-like. We identify an additional source of CP violation in the complex singlet extension compared to the 2HDM, which allows this model a substantially greater freedom in satisfying the stringent EDM constraints. We also incorporate dark matter in this model and investigate the impacts of constraints from the dark sector on the model parameter space and its interplay with CP-violation phases. We further explore the possibility of detecting such a scenario at future collider experiments via CP-violating trilinear couplings among the non-standard scalars. Finally, we also deviate from the exact alignment limit and investigate the CP-properties of the observed Higgs boson in the context of our model. We demonstrate the strong model-dependent nature of the detection prospects of the CP-phase of the Higgs boson at future experiments, exploring both fermion couplings as well as the trilinear self-coupling of the Higgs boson.

  <summary>Details</summary>

In certain cases, the binding energy sharply decreases after considering the recoil corrections. Considering both the $S$\--{}$D$ wave mixing effect and the recoil corrections, we find that recoil corrections, working against the stability of bound states in certain isospin-singlet channels, which cannot be ignored. For the $Ξ_{c}\bar{D}$ and $Ξ_{c}D$ systems with $I(J^P)=0(\frac{1}{2}^{-})$, the $Ξ_{c}\bar{D}^{*}$ and $Ξ_{c}D^{*}$ systems, as well as their bottom counterparts, with $I(J^P)=0(\frac{1}{2}^{-})$ and $0(\frac{3}{2}^{-})$, and the $Λ_{b}\bar{B}^{*}$ system with $I(J^P)=\frac{1}{2}(\frac{1}{2}^{-})$ and $\frac{1}{2}(\frac{3}{2}^{-})$, although the bound state solution can be found both with and without considering the recoil corrections, the inclusion of recoil corrections weakens the attraction of the molecules.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究团队采用了一种基于条件Wasserstein生成对抗网络（CW-GAN）的框架。该模型以输入的中微子能量为条件，使用带有梯度惩罚的Wasserstein损失函数来学习从潜空间到结构化运动学数据的复杂映射。模型针对三种特定的相互作用类型（IBD-CC, NC, NuE-Elastic）在10-31 MeV能量范围内进行训练，直接生成完整的运动学变量，而非降维数据。

Result: 生成的样本在与GENIE测试数据集的对比验证中表现出高度保真度。模型成功复现了所有运动学变量的一维边际分布，并捕捉了它们之间复杂的非线性相关性。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一种可扩展且高效的替代方案，能够为关键的电子中微子相互作用通道提供全谱运动学模拟，同时显著降低了计算开销。

It utilizes a Wasserstein loss function, stabilized by a gradient penalty, to learn the complex mapping from a latent space to structured kinematic data. Our model is tailored to replicate the full multidimensional kinematics of electron neutrino interactions as described by the GENIE event generator. Our focus is specifically on the Inverse Beta Decay (IBD-CC), Neutral Current (NC), and nue-e-elastic scattering processes (NuEElastic), spanning an energy window of 10-31 MeV. Our approach abandons variable reduction schemes and instead generates the entire summary ntuple, enabling holistic event-by-event modeling. Training is performed separately for each of the three interaction types, with rigorous convergence monitoring over 100-300 epochs per channel. We perform a rigorous quantitative validation against held-out GENIE test datasets. The generated samples demonstrate fidelity, reproducing the 1D marginal distributions for all kinematic variables with statistical compatibility, and successfully capturing the complex non-linear correlations between them. This work offers a scalable and efficient alternative to traditional MC event generation, providing full-spectrum kinematic simulation for key electron neutrino interaction channels while drastically reducing computational overhead.

### [118] [Isospin-breaking effects of the double-charm molecular pentaquarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21667)
*Fei-Yu Chen,Ning Li,Wei Chen*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 这篇论文研究了双粲分子态五夸克中的同位旋破缺效应，发现该效应对束缚能有大约10%-30%的显著影响，因此在精确的理论计算中必须考虑此效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究的动机在于，为了使理论计算的精度能够跟上快速发展的实验进展，有必要对奇特强子系统中的同位旋破缺效应进行精确的理论研究。

Method: 该研究使用“单玻色子交换势”（one-boson-exchange potential）框架。通过此方法，研究人员计算了 $D^{(*)}Σ_c^{(*)}$ 系统的束缚性质，以及同位旋 I=1/2 和 I=3/2 态之间的混合角。他们考虑了两种同位旋破缺的来源：一是强相互作用，二是带电组分间的电磁相互作用。

Result: 研究发现，同位旋破缺效应对束缚能的修正贡献达到了约 10% 至 30%，影响显著。这种效应在束缚能较小、半径较大的松散束缚分子态中尤其明显。

Conclusion: 研究结论认为，为了使理论计算的精度与实验进展相匹配，明确地包含同位旋破缺效应是至关重要的。这项研究的结果可以为未来类氘分子态的高精度实验研究提供宝贵的指导。

Abstract: We investigate isospin-breaking effects in double-charm molecular pentaquarks with the $D^{(*)}Σ_c^{(*)}$ configuration, using the one-boson-exchange potential framework. In these systems, the isospin-breaking effects arise from two sources: the strong interaction, which manifests as the threshold difference of the $D^{(*)}Σ_c^{(*)}$ components in the same isospin multiplet and the mass splittings of the exchanged isovector mesons ($π$ and $ρ$); and the electromagnetic interaction between charged $D^{(*)}$ and $Σ_c^{(*)}$ components. We calculate the binding properties and the isospin mixing angle between the $I=1/2$ and $I=3/2$ states of the $D^{(*)}Σ_c^{(*)}$ system. Our results show that the isospin-breaking effect contributes a significant correction of roughly $10\%-30\%$ to the binding energy. This effect is particularly pronounced in loosely bound molecular candidates, which are characterized by small binding energies and large root-mean-square radii. We therefore conclude that the explicit inclusion of isospin-breaking effects is essential for achieving the precision in theoretical calculations necessary to match rapidly advancing experimental programs. Our results are expected to provide valuable guidance for future high-precision experimental studies of deuteron-like molecular states.

### [119] [Strong decays of the hidden-charm molecular pentaquarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21738)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究最近观测到的隐粲五夸克态的强衰变性质，以验证它们的分子态假设，并确定其中一些态的自旋量子数。

Method: 研究采用了分子态框架下的有效拉格朗日方法。通过构建描述五夸克态与其组分强子之间 S 波耦合的有效拉格朗日量，并利用散射 T 矩阵在束缚态极点处的留数来确定耦合常数，从而计算衰变宽度和分支比。

Result: 计算结果显示，衰变宽度对形状因子中的截断参数很敏感，而分支比则不敏感。通过 PψN(4312) 的数据校准参数后，研究倾向于 PψN(4440) 的自旋为 J=3/2，而 PψN(4457) 的自旋为 J=1/2。此外，该模型也能很好地再现 PψsΛ(4338) 和 PψsΛ(4459) 的实验宽度。

Conclusion: 该研究结果支持五夸克态的分子态图像。它为 PψN(4440) 和 PψN(4457) 提供了具体的自旋分配，并成功解释了 PψsΛ 奇特重子偶素的衰变宽度。作者期待未来的实验能够进一步澄清 PψsΛ(4459) 的内部结构。

Abstract: We investigate the strong decays of the recently observed hidden-charm pentaquarks \(P_ψ^N(4312)\), \(P_ψ^N(4440)\), and \(P_ψ^N(4457)\), as well as \(P_{ψs}^Λ(4338)\) and \(P_{ψs}^Λ(4459)\), within the molecular framework using the effective Lagrangian approach. We construct the effective Lagrangians describing the S-wave couplings between these pentaquarks and their constituent hadrons, namely \(Σ_c\bar{D}^{(*)}\) and \(Ξ_c\bar{D}^{(*)}\), and determine the coupling constants via the residues of the scattering \(T\)-matrix at the bound-state poles. Our results show that the decay widths are sensitive to the cutoff parameters in the form factors, whereas the branching fractions exhibit only weak dependence. Using \(P_ψ^N(4312)\) to calibrate the cutoff range, we further explore the spin assignments of \(P_ψ^N(4440)\) and \(P_ψ^N(4457)\). Our calculations favor the assignment where the lower-mass state \(P_ψ^N(4440)\) carries higher spin \(J = 3/2\) and the higher-mass state \(P_ψ^N(4457)\) carries lower spin \(J = 1/2\). In addition, the experimental widths of \(P_{ψs}^Λ(4338)\) and \(P_{ψs}^Λ(4459)\) can both be well reproduced under the molecular interpretation. We look forward to future experimental analyses with more accumulated data to clarify whether the lineshape of \(P_{ψs}^Λ(4459)\) contains contributions from both spin-\(1/2\) and spin-\(3/2\) states.

### [120] [Comparing EPOS-4, EPOS-LHC, and SMASH for identified-hadron observables in the NICA energy range](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21764)
*Murad Badshah,Haifa I. Alrebdi,Sana Raza Khan,Muhammad Ajaz*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 这篇论文使用三种不同的物理模型（EPOS-LHC, EPOS-4, SMASH）模拟了6-8 GeV能量下的金-金碰撞。研究发现，虽然不同模型对普通粒子（如π介子）的预测结果相似，但对奇异粒子（如K介子和Lambda）的预测差异很大，且能量越高差异越明显。这些差异有助于未来实验区分并验证哪种物理模型更准确。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在系统地模拟和研究在低能量金-金（Au+Au）碰撞中（sqrt(sNN) = 6, 7, 8 GeV）可鉴别强子的产生情况。其主要动机是比较三种现代物理模型（EPOS-LHC, EPOS-4, SMASH）的预测能力，并找出能够有效区分这些模型背后不同物理机制的观测量，尤其是在未来NICA实验的能区。

Method: 该研究通过对能量点为 sqrt(sNN) = 6, 7, 8 GeV 的金-金（Au+Au）碰撞进行系统性的模拟。研究采用了三种不同的事件生成框架：EPOS-LHC、EPOS-4（均为混合模型）以及SMASH（纯强子输运模型）。通过比较不同模型生成的各种物理观测量来进行分析，包括快度分布、横动量谱、二维横动量-快度分布、夸克数目定标的椭圆流以及多种粒子产额比。

Result: 模拟结果显示，三种模型对 π 介子的预测大致相似。然而，对于奇异介子和重子，各模型的预测结果差异显著。EPOS-4模型预测的 K+ 和 Lambda 产额最高，且谱形最硬。EPOS-LHC 的结果通常介于两者之间，而 SMASH 模型的奇异粒子产额最低。椭圆流（v2）的分析表明，EPOS-LHC 模型表现出最好的夸克数目定标行为，暗示在该能区存在更强的部分子阶段各向异性。模型之间的差异随能量从6 GeV增加到8 GeV而增大。

Conclusion: 该研究发现，随着碰撞能量从6 GeV增加到8 GeV，不同模型间的预测差异愈发明显。在NICA能区，能够最清晰区分这些模型的观测量是：中等横动量下的重子/介子比率、Lambda/pi+ 比率、横动量对快度的依赖关系、K-/K+ 比率对横动量的依赖关系以及经夸克数目标度的椭圆流 v2。

Abstract: We present a systematic simulation study of identified hadron production in minimum bias Au+Au collisions at sqrt(sNN) = 6, 7, and 8 GeV. The event samples were generated with three modern frameworks based on different microscopic pictures: EPOS-LHC, EPOS-4, and the purely hadronic transport model SMASH. We compare observables that probe baryon stopping, transverse dynamics, hadron formation, and strangeness production: rapidity densities dN/dy, transverse momentum spectra dN/dpT, two dimensional pT-y distributions, v2/nq versus pT/nq, and the yield ratios pi-/pi+, K-/K+, pbar/p, K+/pi+, K-/pi-, p/pi+, and Lambda/pi+.
  For charged and neutral pions, the three models give broadly similar yields and spectral shapes in both dN/dy and dN/dpT. At these energies, resonance decays and isospin constraints reduce the sensitivity to early stage dynamics. In contrast, strange mesons and baryons remain strongly model dependent. EPOS-4 gives the largest midrapidity K+ and Lambda yields and the hardest kaon and strange baryon pT spectra. EPOS-LHC is generally intermediate, while SMASH gives lower strange hadron production. The two dimensional pT-y maps show that the EPOS models populate higher pT over a broader rapidity range. For NCQ scaled elliptic flow, the best approximate scaling is seen in EPOS-LHC, while SMASH and EPOS-4 show only partial scaling. This suggests that EPOS-LHC carries a more coherent partonic anisotropy to the hadronic stage in this energy range. Overall, the model separation grows from 6 to 8 GeV. The clearest discriminators in the NICA domain are intermediate pT baryon to meson ratios, Lambda/pi+, the rapidity dependence of pT, the pT dependence of K-/K+, and NCQ scaled v2.

### [121] [Multiplicity distribution of produced gluons in deep inelastic scattering: main equations and their homotopy solutions for heavy nuclei](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21775)
*Carlos Contreras,Jose Garrido,Eugene Levin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在量子色动力学（QCD）框架下，研究了深度非弹性散射中的粒子多重性分布。作者重新推导了相关截面方程，开发了一种新的“同伦方法”来求解，并最终计算出了高能状态下产生胶子的熵。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在深入理解高能物理中的深度非弹性散射过程，特别是其中产生的粒子（胶子）的多重性分布规律，这是高能量子色动力学（QCD）领域的一个基础性问题。

Method: 1. 在偶极子方法的基础上，重新推导了描述n-切波默子（cut Pomerons）产生截面的方程。
2. 开发了一种“同伦方法”（homotopy approach）来求解这些方程，该方法结合了初次迭代的解析解和后续的数值计算。
3. 利用该方法找到了在n值较大时的解析解。

Result: 1. 新推导出的截面方程与基于AGK切割规则得到的结果相吻合。
2. 成功开发出一种新的求解方法（同伦方法）。
3. 获得了大n值下截面$σ_n$的解析解。
4. 基于此解析解，计算出在高能（大z值）下产生的胶子的熵为 $S_E = \ln(N(z))$。

Conclusion: 论文为深度非弹性散射中的多重性分布问题提供了新的理论推导和创新的求解方案（同伦方法）。研究不仅验证了与现有理论（AGK规则）的一致性，还为特定高能状态下产生的胶子熵提供了明确的解析表达式，为高能QCD现象的理解和计算提供了新工具。

Abstract: In this paper we discuss the multiplicity distribution in the deep inelastic processes in the frame work of high energy QCD. We obtained three results. First, we get the new derivation of the equations for the cross sections of productions of $n$-cut Pomerons in the final states ($σ_n$). These equations coincide with the equations that have been derived using the Abramovsky, Gribov and Kancheli (AGK) cutting rules but based on the dipole approach to QCD. Second, we developed the homotopy approach for finding the solutions to these equations. It consists with the analytic solution for the first iteration and the converge procedure of calculating the next iterations using computing. Third, we found the analytical solution for $σ_n$ at large $n\,\gtrsim\,N(z) = 2 N_0 \,z\,\exp( z^2/(2 κ))$ with $z = \ln( r^2\,Q^2_s )$. Using this solution we calculate the entropy of the produced gluons at large $z$: $S_E = \ln \left( N(z)\right)$, where the saturation momentum $Q_s$ and all constants are discussed in the text.

### [122] [Spacelike and timelike structure functions: a dispersive crossing relation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21779)
*Aniruddha Venkata*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 这篇论文通过一种新的色散关系方法，成功地将深度非弹性散射（DIS）和电子-正电子湮灭（SIA）这两种看似不同的物理过程联系起来，并推导出了描述这两种过程的分布函数与碎裂函数之间的直接关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机源于“交叉对称性”原理，该原理暗示深度非弹性散射（DIS）和半包容性电子-正电子湮灭（SIA）过程之间存在深刻联系。先前的工作（Drell, Levy, and Yan）虽然证明了部分联系，但也指出了继续解析延拓时存在的障碍。本文旨在克服这些障碍。

Method: 作者提出了一种新的关于流相关器（current correlator）解析延拓的色散方案。他们假设多项式有界性，推导出了联系类空和类时截面的减除色散关系。此外，他们引入了一个新的可因式分解的函数来量化交叉障碍，并计算了其最低阶的硬核（hard kernel）。

Result: 研究成功推导出了一个新的恒等式，该恒等式直接将深度非弹性散射中的分布函数与湮灭过程中的碎裂函数联系起来。这为两个不同过程的测量结果提供了直接的理论关联。

Conclusion: 本文通过提出一种新的色散方法，成功克服了先前理论中存在的障碍，建立了深度非弹性散射和电子-正电子湮灭之间更深层次的理论联系。其推导出的分布函数和碎裂函数之间的关系，为连接不同高能物理实验提供了重要的理论基础。

Abstract: Crossing symmetry suggests that deep inelastic scattering and semi inclusive electron-positron annihilation are governed by analytic continuations of a single forward amplitude. Drell, Levy, and Yan proposed that the hadronic tensor admits analytic continuation and demonstrated, in reasonable models, that connected contributions to the cross-section continue. They also identified obstructions to continuation of the current correlator. In this work we supplement their observation with a new dispersive proposal for analytic continuation of the correlator and, assuming polynomial boundedness, derive subtracted dispersion relations relating spacelike and timelike cross sections. We introduce a new factorized function that quantifies the obstruction to crossing and compute its hard kernel at lowest order. The resulting identity connects distribution functions in deep inelastic scattering to fragmentation functions in annihilation.

### [123] [Energy loss predicts no $v_2$ in small systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21861)
*Ben Bert,Coleridge Faraday,W. A. Horowitz*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 一个能量损失模型在小型碰撞系统中，成功预测了粒子产额压低（R_AA），但令人意外地预测椭圆流（v2）几乎为零。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着对小型系统（如O+O、Ne+Ne）碰撞的实验测量取得新进展，研究者们希望检验一个在大型系统中被验证过的能量损失模型是否能够同样解释这些小型系统中的现象，特别是高横动量下的核修正因子（R_AA）和椭圆流（v2）。

Method: 该研究使用了一个结合了逐事件流体动力学演化和小型系统尺寸修正的、基于微扰量子色动力学（pQCD）的能量损失模型。该模型首先在大型系统的实验数据上进行了校准，然后被外推用于预测小型系统的表现。

Result: 模型对Ne+Ne和O+O碰撞中R_AA的预测与近期的实验测量结果在量上吻合。然而，模型预测在所有对称和非对称的小型系统中，高横动量下的v2值都约等于0。

Conclusion: 作者们认为，几乎所有的能量损失模型在使用实验上常用的硬-软关联方法测量时，都会预测v2约等于0。这是因为在小型系统中，产生高能粒子的硬散射过程的参与者平面与产生大部分软粒子的参与者平面之间存在一种普遍的几何去关联。

Abstract: We present high-$p_T$ $R_{AB}$ and $v_2$ from a perturbative quantum chromodynamics-based energy loss model that includes event-by-event hydrodynamic evolution of the medium and small system size corrections to the energy loss. The model is calibrated on, and describes well, large system $R_{AA}$ and $v_2$ experimental data. The extrapolation of our model to $\mathrm{Ne}+\mathrm{Ne}$ and $\mathrm{O}+\mathrm{O}$ agrees quantitatively with recent experimental measurements of $R_{AA}$. Surprisingly, at high-$p_T$ our energy loss model predicts $v_2\approx0$ for all symmetric and asymmetric small systems when extracted using either hard-hard or hard-soft two-particle correlations. We argue that all energy loss models will in general predict $v_2\approx0$ when extracted using hard-soft correlations, which is the usual experimental method for measuring anisotropy in hadronic collisions, due to a generic geometric decorrelation between the hard and soft sector participant planes.

Method: 该研究采用全息方法，通过硬墙和软墙模型分析了在一阶QCD相变过程中，两种不同气泡膨胀情景（Jouguet爆燃和非失控情景）下产生的引力波谱。

Result: 研究发现，增强磁场会使引力波谱的峰值向更低的频率移动。预测的引力波信号强度在IPTA、SKA、BBO和NANOGrav等天文台的可探测范围内。信号分解显示，声波在峰值频率附近占主导地位，气泡碰撞在频谱两端贡献显著，而磁流体湍流的贡献相对较小。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the generation of gravitational waves (GWs) from a first-order QCD confinement-deconfinement phase transition under external magnetic field from holography. We analyze the GWs spectra across both hard wall and soft wall models for Jouguet detonations and non-runaway scenarios. Our results indicate that increasing the magnetic field shifts the spectral peak to lower frequencies. The predicted GWs signals are potentially detectable by observatories such as IPTA, SKA, BBO and NANOGrav. Decomposing the spectra reveals that sound waves typically dominate the signal around the peak frequency, bubble collisions prevail at spectral extremities, and the contribution from MHD turbulence is significant only for non-runaway bubble scenarios at high frequencies. This work suggests that magnetized QCD phase transitions are viable cosmological sources for observable GW backgrounds, offering a potential pathway to constrain primordial magnetic fields through future PTA observations.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该增强框架是一个快速、可靠的工具，能够以远低于全局拟合的计算成本，评估新数据对整体 QCD 参数空间（PDFs 和 $α_s$）的影响，并达到接近全局拟合的精度。

Abstract: We present an extended version of the \texttt{ePump} framework that enables the simultaneous profiling of proton parton distribution functions (PDFs) and the strong coupling $α_s$ using new experimental data. By promoting $α_s$ to a fit parameter within the Hessian updating formalism, the method performs coherent updates of $\{\text{PDFs},α_s\}$ while preserving parameter correlations and the full covariance structure. Validation studies based on CTEQ-TEA analyses with collider data demonstrate that the upgraded \texttt{ePump} accurately reproduces the shifts in PDFs, the preferred $α_s(m_Z)$, and the associated uncertainty reductions obtained in full global fits, including those inferred from Lagrange--Multiplier scans; small deviations arise only for data sets whose $χ^2$ profiles exhibit nonlinear behavior. Applications to representative collider measurements illustrate the impact on the gluon distribution and on precision observables such as the Higgs boson production cross section via gluon fusion. This enhanced framework provides a fast and reliable tool for assessing the effects of new data on the global QCD parameter space, offering near-global-fit accuracy at a fraction of the computational cost.

Motivation: 本文旨在在一个现象学驱动的标准模型扩展（即双希格斯二重态模型, 2HDM）中，验证涡子（vorton）解的可行性。同时，为在计算上更复杂的U(1)对称2HDM中的涡子研究，提供一个计算上易于处理的替代模型。

Method: 研究人员在Z2对称的双希格斯二重态模型（2HDM）中构建了二维的载流环解（扭结涡子）。他们使用细弦近似和弹性弦形式主义来描述这些解，并测试了其在非轴对称扰动下的动态稳定性。此外，他们还识别了一种复合畴壁结构。

Result: 研究发现了多种动态稳定的扭结涡子构型，这些构型在非轴对称扰动下仍然能够保持稳定。研究表明，细弦近似和弹性弦形式主义能高精度地描述这些解，并准确预测其平衡半径和动态振荡频率。此外，他们还发现了一种复合畴壁结构，这为类似扭结涡子的缺陷如何在三维环境中产生提供了可能机制。

Conclusion: 这项工作成功证明了在一种现象学上很重要的标准模型扩展理论（Z2对称2HDM）中，涡子解是可行且稳定存在的。这不仅增强了涡子作为物理现象的可能性，也为研究更复杂的U(1)对称模型中的涡子提供了一个计算上更简便的有效替代方案。

Abstract: We construct and analyse two-dimensional, current-carrying ring solutions, known as kinky vortons, in the $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetric global two-Higgs-doublet model (2HDM). We demonstrate the existence of multiple dynamically stable configurations that persist under non-axially symmetric perturbations. These solutions are described with high accuracy by the thin string approximation and elastic string formalism, which correctly capture both their equilibrium radii and dynamical oscillation frequencies. Kinky vortons in the $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetric theory establish the viability of vorton solutions in a phenomenologically motivated extension of the Standard Model, and should provide a computationally tractable proxy for vortons in the $U(1)$-symmetric 2HDM. In addition, we identify a composite domain wall configuration in which localized condensates are supported on secondary domain walls existing on a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ wall, suggesting a mechanism by which kinky-vorton-like defects could arise in a three dimensional setting.

</details>


### [128] [A perturbative framework to probe infrared sensitivity in non-Abelian gauge theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22072)
*Duarte Fontes,Dennis Horstmann,Kirill Melnikov,Davide Maria Tagliabue*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个新框架，通过希格斯机制引入一个小的胶子质量，来研究QCD中涉及胶子的对撞机过程的红外敏感性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的“重整子模型”无法处理在Born层面就存在胶子的对撞机过程，这限制了对QCD中非微扰功率修正的理解。

Method: 作者将胶子质量提升为一个参数，该参数存在于一个通过希格斯机制自发破缺的非阿贝尔规范场论中。在此框架下，他们在两圈精度下计算了重夸克的极点质量与MS-bar质量之间关系中与胶子质量线性相关的贡献。

Result: 计算出了在两圈精度下，重夸克极点质量与$\overline{\rm MS}$质量之间关系、以及相应场论反项关系中，与胶子质量$m_g$线性相关的贡献。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的框架预计将为探索QCD中对撞机可观测量中的线性红外敏感性提供一个有用的实验平台。

Abstract: Understanding the infrared sensitivity of perturbative predictions in QCD is important for assessing the magnitude of possible non-perturbative power corrections to processes with large momentum transfer. In renormalon models, this sensitivity can be related to computable dependences of perturbative quantities on a small gluon mass. However, this procedure cannot be applied to collider processes with gluons at the Born level. To address this problem, we promote the gluon mass to a parameter of a consistent non-Abelian quantum field theory where the gauge symmetry is spontaneously broken through the Higgs mechanism. Working in the limit in which the gluon mass $m_\mathrm{g}$ is the smallest dimensionful parameter, we compute through two loops the $\mathcal{O}(m_\mathrm{g})$ contributions to the relation between the pole and $\overline{\rm MS}$ masses of a heavy quark and to the relation between corresponding field counterterms. We expect that the proposed framework will provide a useful laboratory for probing linear infrared sensitivity of collider observables in QCD.

</details>


### [129] [The energy-momentum tensor in a classical model of the electron](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22223)
*Grace Gardella,Mira Varma,Peter Schweitzer*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 这篇论文表明，一个经典的电子模型可以成功推导出量子电动力学（QED）中带电粒子能量动量张量（EMT）形状因子的一些关键特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在通过一个清晰且可精确求解的经典模型，来理解和推导量子电动力学（QED）中能量动量张量（EMT）形状因子在小t展开下的非解析项，并对近期提出的质子D-term正则化概念提供见解。

Method: 研究采用了Bialynicki-Birula提出的一个经典电子模型。这个模型是可精确求解的，作者利用它来推导能量动量张量（EMT）形状因子在小t（动量转移平方）展开下的前导非解析项。

Result: 研究成功证明，在量子电动力学（QED）中，带电粒子能量动量张量（EMT）形状因子在小t展开下的前导非解析项，可以通过Bialynicki-Birula的经典电子模型被正确地推导出来。

Conclusion: 该经典模型为理解复杂的量子场论现象提供了一个清晰且有效的途径。此外，基于该模型的清晰性，研究者还对近期提出的质子D-term正则化概念进行了评论，表明该经典方法具有启发性，并可能应用于相关物理问题的研究。

Abstract: We show that the leading non-analytic terms in the small-t expansion of the energy momentum tensor (EMT) form factors of an electrically charged particle in QED can be correctly derived in a classical model of the electron by Bialynicki-Birula. Based on the lucidity of the employed exactly solvable model, we comment also on the recently proposed concept of a regularized proton D-term.

</details>


### [130] [Landau Damping of Collective Neutrino Oscillation Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22246)
*Anson Kost,Huaiyu Duan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文指出，之前报道的稳定快速中微子振荡波的“朗道阻尼”效应，其实际阻尼率非常小，甚至会消失，但这不影响驱动味转换的不稳定模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最近有报告称，集体振荡的稳定快速模式可以通过类似于等离子体波朗道阻尼的机制被阻尼，本研究旨在检验这一说法。

Method: 通过理论分析，重新审视了快速中微子振荡波的阻尼机制。

Result: 研究发现，快速振荡波的实际阻尼率通常非常小，并在纯快速极限下消失。

Conclusion: 此研究结论是，该结果不影响最终驱动超新星和中子星合并中集体中微子味转换的不稳定模式。

Abstract: Dense neutrino media in core-collapse supernovae and neutron star mergers can experience collective flavor transformations in the form of neutrino oscillation waves. It was recently reported that the stable fast modes of collective oscillations can be damped through a mechanism similar to the Landau damping of plasma waves. In this work, we show that the actual damping rates of fast oscillation waves are usually very small and vanishes in the pure fast limit. This result does not affect the unstable modes that eventually drive collective neutrino flavor conversions in supernovae and neutron star mergers.

</details>

### [131] [AlphaLogics: A Market Logic-Driven Multi-Agent System for Scalable and Interpretable Alpha Factor Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20247)
*Zhangyuhua Weng,Shengli Zhang,Taotao Wang,Yihan Xia*

Main category: q-fin.CP

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 AlphaLogics 的多智能体系统，它通过挖掘和生成“市场逻辑”来指导量化因子（alpha factors）的发现，从而提高了因子的预测能力和投资回报。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的因子挖掘技术过于注重发现新的因子，而忽略了其背后的市场逻辑，导致产生的因子复杂、缺乏合理解释且难以规模化。该研究旨在解决这一挑战。

Method: 作者提出了 AlphaLogics 系统，包含三个核心部分：1) 市场逻辑挖掘：从历史因子库中反向提取市场逻辑；2) 因子生成与优化：利用市场逻辑指导生成新因子，并通过回测进行优化；3) 市场逻辑生成与优化：基于现有逻辑库生成新逻辑，并根据其指导的因子表现进行迭代更新。

Result: 在沪深500和标普500指数上的实验表明，AlphaLogics 系统在预测指标和风险调整后收益方面均优于基线模型，并且其生成的市场逻辑库对未来的因子发现也具有实际效用。

Conclusion: 该研究成功构建了一个由市场逻辑驱动的因子挖掘系统（AlphaLogics），它不仅提升了因子的表现，还使得因子背后的逻辑更加清晰、可扩展，为量化投资领域提供了新的研究思路。

Abstract: Factor investing is ultimately grounded in market logic - the latent mechanism behind observed alpha factors that explains why they should persist across assets and regimes. However, recent factor mining prioritizes factor discovery over logic discovery, producing complex alpha factors with unclear rationale, while market logic remains largely handcrafted and difficult to scale.
  To address this challenge, we propose AlphaLogics, a market logic-driven multi-agent system for factor mining. AlphaLogics consists of three key components: (i) Market Logic Mining: reverse-extracting market logic from historical factor libraries to construct an initial market logic library; (ii) Factor Generation and Optimization: using new market logics generated in (i) to guide factor generation, and optimizing factors with backtesting feedback; and (iii) Market Logic Generation and Optimization: generating new market logics conditioned on the initial market logic library, and refining each market logic by aggregating the backtest outcomes of its guided factors, continuously refreshing the library.
  Experiments on CSI 500 and S&P 500 show that AlphaLogics consistently improves predictive metrics and risk-adjusted returns over representative baselines, while producing a market logic library that remains empirically useful for guiding further factor discovery.

</details>
